Current Affairs Commentary

The Start of Negotiations Regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway 15

The Soviet Union has rashly proposed the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway to the puppet state without regard for the wishes of its rightful owner, a point we have repeatedly lamented. Now, this proposal has advanced to formal discussions. While our nation is constrained by military limitations and cannot impose sanctions, it remains uncertain whether Japan and the Soviet Union can achieve substantial progress or whether their diplomacy can transform their previous confrontational stance into a new path. In our estimation, the relationship between Japan and the Soviet Union remains adversarial. Japan's encouragement of the puppet state to negotiate this railway sale stems from a desire to elevate the puppet state's international standing and alleviate its own difficulties. Even if the railway transaction fails, Japan will not suffer any losses. Furthermore, dual diplomacy has always been one of Japan's tactics. By not assuming direct responsibility for this matter, Japan retains greater flexibility. After the commencement of the Soviet-puppet negotiations in Tokyo, the Soviet Union immediately proposed ceding to the Manchurian puppet regime the Chinese Eastern Railway's main and branch lines, totaling 1,069 miles, along with its rolling stock and all other properties. The estimated value is approximately 250 million gold rubles. The Soviet Union's assertion of such a substantial price is based on the fact that the Chinese Eastern Railway is the primary artery connecting Europe and Asia and holds significant political value in northern Manchuria. Once controlled by the puppet state and manipulated by Japan, the political gains would be many times greater than they are today. Secondly, the Chinese Eastern Railway traverses Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces, and the Heilong River basin in northern Manchuria remains largely undeveloped. Considering the economic value along the eastern route, it is still in its nascent stages. Therefore, despite various obstacles such as warfare and floods in the past year, the Chinese Eastern Railway still generated a surplus of over 11 million rubles. Even from a purely economic perspective, it should possess substantial value.

However, the Japanese perspective is quite different. Based on the conditions proposed by their puppet, the price offered to the Soviet Union is merely 50 million Japanese yen, with plans to implement the takeover in three months. Furthermore, they repeatedly assert that Japan will construct a railway network in the three eastern provinces, and with the Jihui Railway nearing completion, the economic value of the Chinese Eastern Railway will soon diminish. Otherwise, Japan could also direct the puppet to forcibly seize the railway, and the Soviet Union would likely be unable to do anything about it. Such is Japan's attitude towards the Soviet Union, viewing the Chinese Eastern Railway as worthless.

Therefore, the transaction for the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, though negotiated by the Soviet Union and the puppet state in Tokyo, has an uncertain outcome at present. However, based on our observation of the general situation, since encompassing the three northeastern provinces, Japan has achieved a temporary military victory, but the stability of Manchuria remains questionable. In terms of international diplomacy, Japan's imperialistic actions have led to increasing isolation. Even the long-standing alliance between Britain and Japan is now facing intense economic competition. The sharp increase in tariffs in India, Australia, South Africa, and other regions is clear evidence of this. The Chinese people's hatred towards Japan is deeply ingrained in the hearts of the general populace, which the Japanese are undoubtedly aware of. Therefore, today, they must make every effort to explore new avenues in diplomacy. In addition to offering sugar-coated poison to our country, they prioritize winning the favor of the Soviet Union. If this Chinese Eastern Railway transaction succeeds, the Soviet Union will not only recognize Japan's seizure of the three northeastern provinces as a fait accompli but will also engage in direct negotiations with the Manchurian puppet regime. Since we cannot impose any practical sanctions, and the Soviet Union recognizes their illegal actions, Japan's gains from aggression will become even more stable. The so-called "Manchukuo" will then acquire a considerable international standing, becoming a second Outer Mongolia. This cannot be considered anything but a diplomatic victory for Japan. The Soviet Union in the Far East will inevitably find itself in an increasingly difficult situation, as its main intention in ceding the Chinese Eastern Railway is to exchange it for peace. Little does it know that Japan, having completed its plan to seize the three northeastern provinces, will implement its continental policy from there. The power of Japanese militarism will continue to grow, and the resources for its military industries will become even more abundant. By applying advanced industrial technology to the development of Manchuria, it is feared that Japan will be able to dominate the Far East and restrict the Soviet Union's development in less than five years. Therefore, the Soviet Union's diplomatic success with Central European countries, even if it achieves peace victories and concludes non-aggression pacts, is merely a facade. It is nothing more than France using the Soviet Union as a barrier to resist the advance of German and Italian fascism, with no genuine love for peace. If, unfortunately, a major war breaks out, and we look back at historical facts, will the so-called sanctity of treaties not be reduced to ashes by artillery fire?

If so, the result of selling the Chinese Eastern Railway will only serve to bolster the viciousness of Japanese imperialism and increase its aggressive flames. The peace hoped for by the Soviet Union will ultimately become illusory, and what will be the position of our country, as the true owner?

The Economic Conference Ends in Failure

Roosevelt's New Declaration Fails to Break the Deadlock

Only an Extension of the Conference, to be Determined by the Steering Committee

Moret Leaves England Last Night to Return Home 16

(London) Another indication of the standstill of the World Economic Conference is the rumored preparation by the conference secretariat to leave on Saturday. (6th Reuters dispatch)

(London) Since the opening of the World Economic Conference, the atmosphere in the conference venue has never been as lively as it is today. The lounges are filled with delegates from various countries and journalists, all speculating about the proceedings of the closed-door meeting of the Steering Committee this morning at 11 o'clock. Many procedures remain to be carried out, and a definitive decision will not be made until the afternoon. As the situation stands, it appears that a plenary session will be convened tomorrow to formally announce the adjournment of the conference, to be reconvened several months later, most likely in Geneva, around October. Professor Moret, a trusted advisor to President Roosevelt, and U.S. Representative Swab will depart London for Plymouth tonight to return to the United States by ship, it is said. (6th Reuters dispatch)

The Steering Committee Discusses Extension Methods 17

The British Prime Minister Proposes a Motion in His Capacity as Chairman

To Avoid Placing Responsibility on Any One Country

(London) The Steering Committee of the Economic Conference, comprising 16 nations – Argentina, Britain, Canada, China, Czechoslovakia, France, Germany, Hungary, Italy, Japan, Mexico, the Netherlands, Spain, Sweden, the United States, and Soviet Russia – met this morning in the Secretariat to discuss methods for extending the conference. The meeting lasted for quite some time, and had not adjourned as of 1 p.m., with no official announcement released.

The British Prime Minister proposed a motion, reportedly by Prime Minister MacDonald in his capacity as Chairman of the Guidance Committee of the conference, to avoid placing the responsibility for the extension on any one country. It is believed that the Steering Committee will continue to meet during lunchtime in an effort to complete its work in one session.

No Results from the Morning Session; It was soon rumored that there were no results, and the meeting was temporarily adjourned to reconvene at 3 p.m. The representatives appeared worried as they left the venue. When reporters asked French Finance Minister Bonnet for his opinion on the future prospects, he merely shrugged his shoulders and declined to answer. Canadian Prime Minister Bennett stated, "I do not believe there is any question of brightness or darkness at present. We are merely adjourning for lunch, and there is nothing beneficial I can say at this time."

The Canadian Prime Minister Opposes the Extension; Mr. Bennett, representing the British autonomous territories, strongly argued that the conference should not be extended. He firmly stated to a Reuters reporter that the conference should not be extended without a vote from the plenary session. However, this opinion was not shared by others, who believed that the Steering Committee's resolution could be implemented without a plenary session. The Economic Conference is not the same as the League of Nations Assembly and has no fixed rules. It is rumored that Prime Minister MacDonald intends to use this point to resolve the dispute in a secret meeting to avoid publicizing the dissenting opinions of various parties, which would hinder the second convocation later this year.

Only Ten Countries Attended; According to the official announcement, only ten of the sixteen countries participating in the Steering Committee's discussions were present: the United States (Hull), Japan (Ishii), Italy (Jang), Sweden (Wigforss), France (Bonnet), Britain (Chamberlain), the Netherlands (Colijn), Canada (Bennett), China (Yan Huiqing), and Spain (Dulwa). It is rumored that this morning's discussions were quite chaotic due to the differing opinions of the representatives. Therefore, the actual outcome is currently difficult to predict.

Hull's Earnest Speech; U.S. Secretary of State Hull delivered an earnest speech, urging the continuation of the conference, stating that the hopes of the world's people rested on their shoulders and that they should not lose heart immediately due to a single setback. This statement was quite effective and garnered the support of Britain, Japan, and the British autonomous territories.

Various Conflicting Opinions; During the Steering Committee's lunchtime adjournment, a draft proposal was discussed to allow the work of various committees to continue as usual, except for the monetary and related issues. Several members of the Steering Committee had lunch at the U.S. Embassy and continued these discussions. Regarding the opposition to the immediate extension without holding a plenary session, a compromise solution has been proposed to expand the Steering Committee by adding the chairmen of various committees. However, it seems absolutely certain that the entire conference will be extended, and not just the monetary committee, although some committees will not be affected. The Exchange Market Unaffected; The breakdown of the conference seems to have had no impact on the exchange market. The U.S. dollar opened today at 4.50 yuan, then returned to 4.475 yuan, but soon fell again to 4.505 yuan. Gold coins remained strong. (6th Reuters dispatch)

(London) The Steering Committee of the Economic Conference met this morning at 10 o'clock and adjourned at 1:30 p.m. to reconvene at 4 p.m. for a final decision on the fate of the conference.

Like Jurors Deadlocked; When the meeting opened this morning, the members were like jurors who had reached a deadlock, but ham toast and fine wine were summoned several times. However, according to reporters, none of the sixteen members publicly advocated for a formal adjournment.

Chamberlain's Proposal; British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain attempted to break the deadlock by proposing a draft resolution suggesting (1) that various committees and subcommittees continue their work, decide what they can accomplish, and then report to the Economic and Monetary Committees; (2) that a plenary session be convened before the end of July; and (3) that the Steering Committee continue to meet once a week.

Rejected by Italy and France; French Finance Minister Bonnet and Italian Foreign Minister Janck both directly rejected Chamberlain's plan. However, both men, representing gold standard countries, declared their opposition to a formal adjournment and their support for continuing the conference, insisting that monetary issues and other related issues such as tariffs not be discussed further.

Our Country's Position; In addition, Chinese representative Yan Huiqing, Japanese chief representative Ishii, Dutch Minister Colijn, Swedish representative Wigforss, and Spanish representative Dulwa also delivered speeches. China and Japan both supported continuing the conference.

A Drafting Committee Was Elected; Before the adjournment, a drafting subcommittee was elected to prepare a written proposal to be presented at the Steering Committee meeting at 4 p.m. Both supporters and opponents of Chamberlain's proposal were selected for the drafting committee. Seeking a Reasonable Approach; It is reported that there is general agreement within the Steering Committee that the conference should continue if a satisfactory way to remove the current obstacles can be found. Currently, this approach is being sought by the drafting committee. According to the majority opinion, the most reasonable approach would be to allow the Economic and Monetary Committees to independently decide their own procedures, so that the Monetary Committee could temporarily adjourn and the Economic Committee could proceed freely. (6th National Telegraph)

President Roosevelt's New Declaration

Reiterates That Monetary Issues Are Not the Fundamental Objective at Present

Determined to Cooperate with the Conference to First Seek the Recovery of World Prices

Urgent Stability of Currency Values Artificially

May Hinder the Country's Economic Recovery

The U.S. Has Not Yet Reached the Time to Return to the Gold Standard

Will Retain the Right to Choose the Future

(Washington) President Roosevelt issued a declaration today, which has been telegraphed to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol. The declaration states that the President wishes the World Economic Conference to continue, and that the temporary disputes over stabilizing currency values cannot diminish the suitability of this discussion. The Conference should urgently seek to alleviate and remedy the pains of the current economic situation. The United States is determined to cooperate, and the revaluation of the gold standard for American goods is an objective that cannot be passively changed by the American public. Today, the United States has no intention of determining the value of the gold standard based on foreign currencies. In addition to stabilizing currency values, other major issues should also be explored. The primary task is to restore prices so that they are profitable and efficient for industrial and agricultural operations. The needs and policies of various countries do not necessarily align. Stabilizing their currency values uniformly today would be artificial and unrealistic, and may hinder other countries from realizing the policies necessary for their domestic prosperity. The declaration also clearly states that the United States' policies do not harm the interests of any country. It concludes by saying that when European currency values were lowered, the United States had no complaints. Like Britain, the United States views the restoration of the gold standard as its ultimate goal, but it must choose its own time and ratio. (5th Reuters dispatch)

(London) President Roosevelt's new declaration, telegraphed to Hull, states that the final exchange rate of the American gold standard depends on the success of other countries in raising prices. To achieve success in raising prices, the increased prices must be periodic currency units rather than other separately agreed units. Therefore, such prices cannot be predetermined. President Roosevelt then pointed out that the United States has never criticized France, Italy, and Belgium for adopting the policy of devaluing their currencies and has expressed sympathetic understanding for Britain and Scandinavia's abandonment of the gold standard. He declared that the United States fully agrees with the British government's statement in the House of Commons that Britain reserves the right to choose the timing of its return to the gold standard and the ratio of gold to its restoration. President Roosevelt also stated that the United States does not attempt to persuade various countries to adopt any particular domestic policy but maintains that the Economic Conference should lead the restoration of prices to a beneficial level and then maintain the stable prices obtained at this time. (5th National Telegraph)

European Gold Standard Countries Unanimously Support the Extension 18

Threatening to Withdraw from the Tariff Truce

(London) The Gold Standard countries held a meeting last night and unanimously passed a resolution to support the extension of the Economic Conference. This move by the Gold Standard countries will ensure that the Steering Committee's meeting today will resolve to extend the conference. The Gold Standard countries met at the French delegation's office for an hour and a half before reaching this decision. After the meeting, it was heard from the French legal circles that, in the opinion of the Gold Standard countries, President Roosevelt's recent remarks, although making substantial progress, confirmed the Gold Standard countries' opinion that there are differences in monetary concepts between Europe and the United States, and it is difficult to seriously continue the work of the conference at present. However, the Gold Standard countries felt that President Roosevelt's remarks this time did have the intention of expecting closer and sympathetic cooperation, which was not found in previous American declarations. This time, the wording was very moderate, which could facilitate the continuation of future conference affairs after the extension of the conference. As for the issue of how long to extend the conference, the Gold Standard countries did not discuss it, as they felt that the currency issue could not be given a deadline. From the Gold Standard countries' point of view, the future changes in the U.S. dollar must be closely monitored. (6th Reuters dispatch)

(London) European representatives have failed to observe the American attitude in the same light. After the gold standard countries' representatives met at midnight today to discuss response plans, the French representatives immediately declared that the Economic Conference would be adjourned on Thursday. It is heard that several countries' representatives have notified secretaries and typists to prepare to leave London on Saturday. Although the adjournment plan has not yet been finalized, it is now believed that the Steering Committee will be asked to reconvene within 60 days to consider whether it is possible to reopen the conference. The representatives are not entirely in favor of adjournment, and the meeting is currently divided into two factions. (5th National Telegraph)

(London) After seeing the U.S. President's final declaration, the representatives of the gold standard countries all believe that the Economic Conference has little hope of continuing and have declared that they will withdraw from the tariff truce of May 12 and return to a protectionist economic policy. (6th National Telegraph)

The Gold Standard Countries Unite 19

Representatives of Various National Banks

Will Meet in Paris Tomorrow

(Paris) A meeting of countries adhering to the gold standard system will be held in Paris on Saturday, chaired by Moreau, Governor of the Bank of France. Participants will include the leaders of the central banks of Belgium, the Netherlands, Switzerland, Italy, and Poland. The meeting will discuss the situation created by the United States' adoption of a position on currency stability and methods to curb speculation. The meeting will be purely for the exchange of views, and the actions of the representatives at the meeting will not bind the governments. Talks between the governments will take place after the meeting. (6th Havas dispatch)

Terpstra, Governor of the Netherlands National Bank in The Hague, announced again today that the Netherlands is determined to maintain the gold standard. Mr. Terpstra expressed his deep understanding of President Roosevelt's attitude expressed from the American position, saying that the U.S. President's primary concern is to protect the interests of the American business community. Conversely, as the Governor of the Netherlands National Bank, he should support the gold standard countries' plan, as these countries see currency stability as necessary for restoring world trade. (6th National Telegraph)

(London) The Free City of Danzig has joined the gold group and has now formally announced its participation in the declaration of the European gold standard countries on July 3 to maintain the gold standard. It has also instructed the Danzig Central Bank to contact the central banks of the gold standard countries in order to actively implement this declaration. (6th Reuters dispatch)

Britain and the United States Prepare to Revert to Economic Nationalism 20

The U.S. Will Increase Tariffs to Restrict Imports

The British Industries League Opens an Imperial Economic Conference

(London) The Imperial Committee of the British Industries Federation has unanimously passed a recommendation advocating that an Imperial Economic Conference be convened in London in the event that the Economic Conference fails. (5th Havas dispatch)

(Washington) Tonight, after hearing the news that the U.S. President will soon prohibit the import of certain foreign goods, and that the Imperial Committee of the British Industries Federation has recommended reopening the Imperial Economic Conference after the failure of the Economic Conference, there are deep fears that Britain and the United States will completely revert to economic nationalism. After today's cabinet meeting, it was announced that the U.S. President will convene a meeting with the Director of Industrial Recovery, Johnson, and the Secretary of Commerce, Roper, on Thursday to discuss industrial policy. According to sources close to the President, he intends to shorten working hours, increase wages, and restrict production to meet national needs. If so, the import of foreign goods would be sufficient to hinder the success of this plan. Therefore, informed sources expect the President to soon impose additional tariffs on certain goods and prohibit the import of certain goods. (5th National Telegraph)

(Washington) The United States joined the League of Nations' 1927 convention on the abolition of import prohibitions and restrictions. The Washington government has recently notified the League of Nations that the United States is withdrawing from this convention. The U.S. government's intention is that this convention may hinder the plan to restore the domestic economy of the United States, and the State Department also believes that this convention has been ineffective up to now. Its declaration of withdrawal is due to this. (5th Havas dispatch)

Representatives of Wheat-Producing Countries Draft an Adjustment Plan 21

(London) Representatives of wheat-producing countries decided today to draft a plan to adjust wheat production and limit the acreage of wheat cultivation in consuming countries, but it is expected that this draft will be submitted for review in the future, during the dangerous period of negotiations to restrict wheat production. (5th National Telegraph)

Air Defense Exercise Held in Tokyo 22

(Tokyo) The Tokyo area will hold a four-day air defense exercise starting on August 9. According to the plan announced today, railway personnel in the Chiba area must participate in detecting the arrival of enemy aircraft, and the windows of all night trains must be equipped with curtains so that enemy aircraft cannot easily see in. When the train enters a designated location, passengers must lower the curtains themselves. The Tokyo Railway Administration has issued a notice asking all passengers to cooperate to ensure the success of the air defense exercise. (6th Reuters dispatch)

Page 9

Premier Wang Issues a Statement

The Whole Country Should Have a Common Will and Unify Against External Forces

The Dalian Negotiations Still Adhere to the Principles of the Tanggu Truce

The Government Is Considering Concluding a Non-Aggression Treaty with Russia

Nanjing Wang Jingwei talked about, ㈠ After the signing of the Sino-Japanese ceasefire agreement, the rumors that Japan's plan to invade China intends to expand North China as a political and economic base are only seen in newspapers. Whether they are true remains to be verified. At this time of crisis, all leaders in the country should have a common will to strengthen national power and unite against external forces. Japan takes advantage of the disunity and differing political views of our country's leaders to sow discord. If foreign troubles are pressing, national power cannot be strengthened, and will cannot be unified, how can we talk about resistance, let alone friendliness? At this time, the people of the country should share weal and woe and unite for survival in order to save the current crisis. ㈡ The scope of the Dalian negotiations is limited to the restoration of traffic and the police guarding the railways.

However, Japan has violated the principles of the Tanggu Truce and made two unreasonable demands, which have naturally been rejected. This matter has been entrusted to the Pingzheng Committee and the Ping Military Branch to handle cautiously in accordance with the central government's intentions and the principles of the Tanggu Truce. We received a report last night that the Japanese side has room for change. In short, as long as the Japanese side does not violate the Tanggu Truce, there is the possibility of further discussions. ㈢ The free movement of the three warships Haiqi, Zhaohe, and Haishen is also an unfortunate event. The report states that they have already arrived in Hong Kong, and the central government is now sending a telegram to recall them and transfer them to the central government's command in order to unify the navy and ensure that the navy's strength is no longer divided. Therefore, after Mayor Shen resigned as the commander of the Northeast Fleet, it seems unnecessary to appoint another candidate. ㈣ The war between the two Lius is extremely distressing, and the alarms of the Red Disaster in northern Sichuan are frequent.

Both sides should cease fighting as soon as possible to save the crisis. Chairman Jiang has already telegraphed both sides to immediately return to their original defenses and restore the pre-war state. The Executive Yuan advocates continuing to proceed based on the four measures for governing Sichuan previously established to enable both sides to cease fighting and jointly suppress the bandits. ㈤ The government is still considering the mutual non-aggression and security pacts signed by the Soviet Russian government and its neighboring countries, and no decision has been made yet on whether or not to join them. ㈥ The nation's Chinese-owned yarn factories have all suspended night work due to sluggish sales, and labor-management disputes are bound to arise again. The central government is studying a method that takes into account the interests of both labor and management to provide relief. ㈦ The sudden adjournment of the World Economic Conference held in London is shocking. This conference is of great importance to the stability of the world's finance, so it is highly valued by all countries in the world. ㈧ The affairs of Chahar Province are entirely handled by the Pingzheng Committee and the Ping Military Branch nearby.

So far, they have embraced the four words of peaceful handling. ㈨ The central government attaches great importance to the claim that the puppet state has allocated more than 13 million yuan to suppress the volunteer armies. The volunteer armies hiding in Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang are numerous and are a real worry for the rebels. However, judging from the situation, it will not be easy. (6th Special Telegraph)

The Hangzhou Northeast Aviation School has been ordered by the Military Affairs Commission to merge with the Central Aviation School. All 77 officers and students have been sent to Hangzhou for training. After examination and screening, 11 of those who passed the physical examination for flight officers were approved to serve as instructors, 8 were approved to serve as instructors, 19 failed, 17 of the students passed, and 22 failed. Those who failed will be transferred to the Central Military Academy for military training. Shen Desie, Director of the Military Affairs Department of the Aviation Administration, has been specially appointed to go to Beiping to take over all aircraft and other equipment of the Northeast Aviation School. Shaanxi Disaster Still Awaiting Relief 26

The Ministry of Railways in Nanjing previously charged half price for the transport of flour to Tongguan via the Pinghan, Jinpu, and Longhai railways due to the severe famine in Shaanxi. It is proposed to extend the reduced price transport of flour to Tongguan for another two months. The Ministry of Railways has approved this. (6th Dispatch)

Control Yuan Dispatches Personnel to Various Provinces for Inspection 27

The Control Yuan in Nanjing has dispatched Gao Yihan, Liu San, Shao Hongji, Zhou Lisheng, Liu Eqing, and Gao You Tang, six individuals in total, to various provinces including Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, and Hebei to inspect various matters including war damage, banditry, disaster victims, dike construction, and prisons. Each person receives a monthly travel allowance of 300 yuan. The inspection period is one month, with departures scheduled one after another within three days. (6th Dispatch)

Rumors of Huang Musong Being Under Surveillance 28

Liu and Sheng Telegraph to Nanjing Explaining Emergency Measures

Gong and Peng to Fly to Xinjiang on the 11th

Following the news of the execution of Tao Mingyue, the Secretary-General of the new Xinjiang provincial government in Nanjing, rumors spread in the capital that Huang Musong, the Special Envoy, was under surveillance. Inquiries with personnel from the new Xinjiang provincial government stationed in Nanjing revealed that this was not the case. Gong Bicheng stated that the matter was a false rumor. However, the Nanjing office of the Special Envoy's office stated that Huang was placed under "invisible surveillance" upon arriving in Xinjiang and that the office had not received any telegrams from Huang since the 28th. They also claimed that outgoing telegrams may not have reached him, suggesting that his surveillance was undoubtedly true. Another report stated that Huang recently sent a telegram to a friend in Nanjing, requesting that they urge the government to appoint Liu Wenlong as Chairman and Sheng Shicai as Military Governor, so that the Special Envoy's mission could be easily completed. He also requested that they contact an airline to arrange for a plane to come so that he could return east. (6th Dispatch)

Gong Bicheng from Nanjing said that he and Peng Zhaoxian are scheduled to fly to Xinjiang on the 11th. The central government has ordered Huang Musong to return to Nanjing as quickly as possible. Liu and Sheng are supported by the people and are in charge of military and political affairs, so they are still able to live together in harmony. The central government was extremely shocked when it received the news from the new Xinjiang authorities about the execution of Tao Mingyue and others. It immediately telegraphed Liu and Sheng, instructing them to act cautiously. A reply was received on the 6th, stating that this action was an emergency measure. The new province of Xinjiang would still follow the instructions of the central government. In his personal opinion, Gong believed that Xinjiang is related to border defense. Improper handling could invite foreign aggression, so caution is necessary. (6th Dispatch)

Huang Musong of Nanjing telegraphed Wang on the 6th, replying that he will return to Nanjing by Eurasia plane within the next few days. (6th Dispatch)

An official in Nanjing said that since the previous incident in Xinjiang, the central government believed that it was extremely important to eliminate the situation in Xinjiang as soon as possible, as the country was facing a serious national crisis. Chiang and Wang repeatedly exchanged telegrams to discuss the matter before deciding to send Huang Musong as a Special Envoy. Since arriving in Xinjiang, Huang has not been surrounded by any party or protected any one side to create a certain faction. Unexpectedly, someone took hold of Huang's name as Special Envoy and suppressed everything, resulting in the killing of three important officials. Wang summoned Zhang Mingjiu and Gong Bicheng to discuss the matter. In addition to telegraphing Liu and Sheng not to escalate the situation, Gong Bicheng and Peng Zhaoxian were ordered to go to Xinjiang as soon as possible to investigate the truth. During the Central Standing Committee meeting on the 7th, the members had a detailed discussion and still adhered to the principle of peace to determine an appropriate solution. As for the government's telegram urging Huang Musong to return to Nanjing, it was sent on the 5th. It is reported that Huang will wait for Gong and Peng to arrive in Xinjiang, consult with them briefly, and then return to Nanjing. (6th Dispatch)

Zhang Mingjiu, the director of the Xinjiang Provincial Government's office in Nanjing, is scheduled to go to Jiangxi on the 7th to meet with Chiang, report on the recent handling of Tao Mingyue and others by the new Xinjiang provincial government, and ask Chiang for his opinion on the Xinjiang situation in order to resolve it quickly and avoid a stalemate. (6th Dispatch)

Bai Tianmin Discusses the Battle of Yihuang 29

Bai Tianmin, the Brigade Commander who stubbornly defended Yihuang, arrived in Nanchang Hospital from the front line on the 5th due to a foot injury. Before his hospitalization, Bai discussed the battle with a reporter from the Central News Agency as follows: His brigade was ordered to depart on the 3rd of last month, arrived in Yihuang on the 4th, took over defense on the 5th, and encountered bandit ambush on the 6th. He led his troops to meet the enemy. The bandits, seeing our weakness, attacked with all their forces, so he decided to enter the city and defend it to the death. At that time, the main force of the bandits launched a fierce attack on them, lasting three days and nights, without success. They then mobilized the pseudo-5th Army Corps to encircle and attack, and the pseudo-1st Army Corps changed to harass Fuzhou. The bandit army planned to capture Yihuang and Chongren, take Fuzhou, and then advance south to Nanchang. Only 2,000 people were defending the city, so while requesting assistance, they resisted the enemy. The siege was only relieved when reinforcements arrived. Recalling the period of encirclement, the bandits attacked every day, with seven major battles and countless minor battles. It is estimated that the bandits lost one division commander, two regimental commanders, and over 3,000 soldiers. They suffered over 600 casualties among officers and soldiers. He was also injured because he encouraged his subordinates to fight the bandits to the death. He will return to the defense line to kill bandits after his injury heals. (Central News Agency Report, 6th)

Huai River Conservancy Association Prevents the Yellow River from Shifting into the Huai River 30

The lower reaches of the Yellow River in southern Shandong have recently become increasingly silted up, showing signs of shifting into the Huai River. The Huai River Conservancy Association is concerned that if this happens, the Huai River governance project will suffer a major blow. It has submitted a request to the National Government to find a way to prevent the shift into the Huai River. The government has ordered that temporary measures be taken to prevent siltation in the lower reaches of the Yellow River. The association has now decided to intensify the prevention of siltation in southern Shandong and dredge the river channels. At the same time, it will also make arrangements to take care of the upstream projects of the Yellow River to prevent problems before they occur. (6th Dispatch)

US Ambassador to Sweden Ordered to

Investigate Russian Business and Political Situation

(National Report, 5th)

London - The new US Ambassador to Sweden, Steinhardt, passed through here today on his way to Stockholm to take office. He is tasked with informally studying the issue of US recognition of the Soviet Union, paying particular attention to communist propaganda and Russian debts to the US. Russia owes the US a total of 57.3 million US dollars, of which 40 million US dollars were borrowed during the Tsarist era, and the remainder was owed by the Kerensky Provisional Government. The Soviet government denied this debt after its establishment. Soviet Western Border Consolidated 44

London, 5th - According to a National Dispatch, the treaty between the Soviet Union and Lithuania interpreting the meaning of "aggressor" was signed today at the Soviet Embassy in London by Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov and Lithuanian Ambassador to London, Jurgis Šaulys. This treaty is the same in intent and wording as the treaty signed by the Soviet Union with other countries on July 3rd. The reason why the Soviet Union signed this treaty separately with Lithuania this time is that Lithuania and Poland have been in a state of diplomatic rupture for several years, so the two countries could not sign the same treaty text. Now that this organization of peace treaties is in place, the entire western border of the Soviet Union will not be subject to any unwarranted aggression.

British Parliament Discusses China-Japan Issue 48

(London) Tonight, during the House of Commons debate on the Foreign Affairs Budget, Opposition Leader Lansbury strongly criticized Japan's policy in the Far East. Lansbury asked, "Who is now protecting the interests of British nationals in 'Manchukuo'? Japan has torn up various treaties, swept through Manchuria, and advanced!" Former Foreign Secretary Austen Chamberlain rose and declared that Lansbury was too focused on League of Nations sanctions and that he himself wished to focus on preventing mistakes. When the Far Eastern incident occurred, he expressed his deep sympathy for Japan. He felt that the League of Nations was too unsympathetic to the difficulties Japan faced due to internal unrest in China. However, after the incident was prolonged, we dare to conclude that Japan itself has greatly increased its mistakes. Its actions in Manchuria are in direct contradiction to the three solemn international treaties it has signed. Chamberlain then asked the government whether the recommendations of the Lytton Commission could not be applied to "Manchukuo" so as to cause no loss to Japanese interests and Chinese sovereignty. (Reuters Report, 5th)

(London) Former Foreign Secretary Austen Chamberlain spoke out against Germany's treatment of Jews during the House of Commons debate on the Foreign Affairs Budget tonight, saying, "How can Britain remain friends with a country that treats another nation outside the protection of the law because of racial relations?" The spirit expressed by Germany is harmful to any country outside its borders and to any nation in Germany's future colonies. Unless Germany expresses a moderate and appropriate way that it can accept to revise the Treaty of Versailles, anyone who allows Germany to consider any modification as possible is an enemy of peace. Conservative Party member Rune expressed the opinion that China could welcome any friendly act that would help it reorganize its government. Cannot the United States, Japan, France, and Britain unite to do something? Undersecretary of State Eden replied to Lansbury, saying that the League of Nations has no reason to be ashamed of its performance. The League of Nations is not an emperor and cannot exceed its authority. As for the arms embargo on the Far East, all countries do not have equal legislative power to strictly enforce the embargo. All countries must have this power before a unified ban on arms exports can be considered. As for Britain's interests in Manchuria, although Britain has not recognized "Manchukuo," it has stationed consular staff. Eden went on to talk about disarmament, acknowledging that there are indeed dangers in signing a disarmament convention at the moment, but said that there are also dangers in not agreeing to this convention. Therefore, Europe must first be comforted to have sufficient trust to sign this convention. This matter requires the assistance of all of Europe, and the assistance of countries that speak of unequal status is especially important. Foreign Minister Simon, in concluding the debate, spoke of the war debts owed to the United States, saying that negotiations would be held soon, but the date had not yet been determined. The negotiations will cover the entire war debt, not just one installment of the debt. The US President has already explained this. The UK and the US are now going to revise the existing agreements to adapt to the recovery of prosperity. (Reuters Report, 5th)

Specific Plans for Japan's Annexation of Manchurian Industry 51

Plans Divided into Four Major Categories, to be Implemented Starting This Summer

Manchuria Road Construction Costs 150.5 Million Yuan

July 1st, Tokyo Nichi Nichi Shimbun reported: "Since the economic construction of 'Manchukuo' has been intensively studied by authorities in various fields, all major industries have been brought under a certain degree of control, and it has been decided to implement them all starting this summer. The specific plan is as follows: ㈠ Controlled Enterprises: All major industries will be transferred to joint operation by Japan and 'Manchukuo', that is, 'Manchukuo' will use existing goods as collateral for funds, and Japan will provide funds. There are seven important enterprises: 1. Manchuria Gasoline Company: Establish a gasoline company to purchase refined crude oil and heavy oil. 2. Manchuria Coal Mine Company: Merge the major coal mines in Manchuria into a joint Japanese-Manchurian enterprise. Fushun and Benxihu will not join for the time being, and will be merged later. Set up a head office in Changchun. 3. Japan-Manchuria Mineral Company: Mainly based on products from Manchuria, and jointly operated with companies in Niigata Prefecture, Japan. Also, establish an industrial company to conduct large-scale industrial experiments. 4. Ammonium Sulfate Industry Company: The Manchuria Chemical Industry Company has already been established, and a testing ground is being prepared in Dalian. 5. Manchuria Electric Power Company: In order to control Manchurian electricity, a joint Japanese-Manchurian electric power company will be established with its head office in Changchun. 6. Manchuria Gold Mining Company: Establish a joint Japanese-Manchurian gold mining company to operate gold mining businesses in Heilongjiang, Xing'an Province, and Jilin Province. 7. Alcohol Company: Because the alcohol business in Harbin has always suffered from overproduction, a joint Japanese-Manchurian company will be established to control the industry. ㈡ Privately Operated Enterprises: There are eight enterprises that Japanese and Manchurians have already started to operate or are planning: 1. Cement Company: Except for the control of production volume, factory location, and sales area, private businesses are allowed to operate freely. 2. Jute Manufacturing Company: Planning a jute manufacturing business in northern Manchuria. 3. Public Bus Business: This business is allowed to be operated by private businesses, as long as it does not directly interfere with the railway. 4. Brewing Business: Preparing to establish a Japanese sake brewery in the Tiexi industrial zone of Fengtian. 5. Animal Husbandry Business: Preparing to operate a large-scale animal husbandry business. 6. Entrusted Operation of State-owned Placer Gold Mining Areas: Those with definite capital are allowed to operate. 7. Fiber Paper Manufacturing Business: This is the business with the greatest hope from the private sector. 8. Farms: Many are preparing to operate large farms, mostly Koreans, using Manchurian farmers. ㈢ Planned Enterprises: There are also four items currently being planned for controlled economy: 1. Forest Development Company: A joint Japanese-Manchurian enterprise for logging large forests in Jilin Province and transplanting trees, etc. 2. Horse and Sheep Business: Actively studying and implementing methods for the controlled planning of horse and sheep breeding. 3. Salt Manufacturing Business: Increase the salt fields in the Yingkou area, reduce the price of salt in Manchuria, and supply industrial salt to Japan. 4. Pharmaceutical Manufacturing Business: Planning to manufacture special drugs such as morphine and paralytic gokoku under control. ㈣ Immigration Business: 1. In the vicinity of Qihuli in the south of Jiamusi (i.e., the south of the first immigration area), another 500 self-defense immigrants will be sent in mid-July. 2. The area along the Jidun-Duntu line was originally an important transportation line for national security and defense, and a family self-defense immigration plan is being planned. 3. Other free immigrants: There are also various plans, and all are permitted as long as they comply with the general guidelines. On the other hand, a large-scale immigration subsidy agency is being established in Japan. Currently, an immigration association is being established to raise 2 million yuan in funds.

According to Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, Manchuria's roads are the worst in the world. Since the establishment of the National Highway Bureau on March 3 this year, the total length of planned roads has reached 60,000 kilometers, with a cost of 150.5 million yuan. It is planned to be carried out in ten years, with two phases of construction. The first phase is five years for 34,000 kilometers, and it is planned to complete 4,000 kilometers this year and 3,300 kilometers next year. The goal of the national highway is to take Changchun as the center and connect major cities and important cities with each other and with county towns to facilitate national defense and industry. The regulations stipulate that first-class roads should be 7 meters wide, second-class roads should be 6 meters wide, and the following belong to third-class roads. First- and second-class roads are for motor vehicles, but in river areas, due to the uncertain changes in rivers, those who cannot build bridges should lay stones on the riverbed in shallow water, and use ferries in deep water. In the Xing'an Province and other large plains, road signs will be built. Construction has already started between Fengtian and Fushun, and between Changchun and Jilin. Labor is mainly recruited from local people, and in order to prevent the deterioration of vagrants and relieve unemployment, military engineers are building roads.

Deng Xihou Counterattacks Liu Wenhui 52

Liu Xiang Strives to Unify Various Armies

Troops of the Two Lius Have Not Yet Made Contact

Chongqing Correspondence: Since Liu Xiang decided to use force to stop the Sichuan War, the atmosphere has suddenly become tense. At the same time, troops under Liu's command who were ordered to join the suppression of bandits in northern Sichuan have also been mobilized one after another. There is a phenomenon in the Sichuan army that is worth noting. The previously fragmented troops of various departments have gradually unified their orders. Although Yang Sen had previously established his own banner, he has recently returned to Liu's command. The troops of Tian Songyao and Deng Xihou also had independence in the past, but since Liu Wenhui and Deng Tian had a conflict last year, Deng Tian, unable to resist Wenhui alone, also attached themselves to Liu Xiang one after another. Tian's military pay is now completely collected in Chongqing, and he listens to Liu Xiang's dispatch. This time, Liu and Deng have another conflict, and Deng expresses more obedience to Liu Xiang. Deng's army number has now been completely reorganized in accordance with Chongqing. This is the manifestation of the fact. Therefore, the only one who is unwilling to attach to Yu is Liu Wenhui's

80,000 people, while the remaining 180,000 people are all under Liu Xiang's command. Therefore, the result of this re-battle between the two Lius may lead to the unification of military power in Sichuan. As for the troops of the two Lius, as of the time of sending the message, they have not yet made contact, because the rear deployments have not yet been finalized. Although Liu Wenhui had issued a telegram advocating joint suppression of the Red Army, this is just a kind of advertisement that usually precedes the start of a war. In fact, he has appointed six command routes and appointed Ding Xiangyuren as the commander of the rear guard. These are all wartime names, which shows that the war is on the verge of breaking out. Luo Zezhou, Li Qixiang, and other generals issued a Jiang telegram to Liu Wenhui today (3rd), stating that the Red Disaster and civil unrest are worrying, and asked Provincial Liu to repent and withdraw his troops back to defense, return the defense area and occupied agencies of Deng's troops, and allocate two divisions of troops to cooperate with the various armies to suppress the Red Army, under the unified command of Liu Xiang, and proceed as a whole, otherwise the various armies will cooperate to remove obstacles in order to suppress bandits. From this, it is also conceivable that the various troops of Luo and Li are ready to use force against Wenhui.

At this juncture, what is the situation of the Sichuan bandits is worth noting. According to the latest reports, Xu Xiangqian's bandit troops are still controlling the county borders of Tongnanba, and have not attacked, and are trying to concentrate property and coerce the people. Tian Songyao's troops are still guarding the south bank of the three rivers of Cangxi Guozhong Yilong and Guangyuan and have not counterattacked. In Suifu Hongkou, there are more than a thousand Red bandits attacking Huangzhongbao. This place is Liu Cunhou's defense line. After Liu ordered Liao Zhen's troops to suppress them with two regiments, the bandits had retreated on the 29th. Both soldiers and bandits suffered casualties in this battle. About 300 soldiers were killed or injured. The He bandits between Sichuan and Hubei are still distributed in Changtan River, Hongtuxi, and Qianzhan Dam. Xu Yuanquan is instructing Jiang and Zhang's troops to find the main force of the bandits in preparation for an attack. According to telegrams obtained by the military department here, Xu himself had returned to Yichang from Shinan today (3rd).

The anti-tax army in southern Sichuan is still strong. County Magistrate Chen of Qionglai County has been captured and killed by them. The people in Chengdu are restless and the security is worrying. Deng Xihou's residence in the province was robbed on the evening of the first of this month, and the son of Kou, the director of his military supplies office, was kidnapped. His whereabouts are unknown. The streets are closed to pedestrians at 8 pm. The troops stationed in the province, Shi Zhaowu and Zhu Zhizhao, have always been lax in discipline, and recently, due to the difficulty in paying salaries, they have even more outrageous actions, but no one dares to intervene. Deng Xihou himself has gone to Jintang to supervise the army, and began to counterattack Banzhuyuan, Zhaojiadu, and other places yesterday (2nd), and fierce battles have occurred. (July 3rd)

Qingdao Various Circles Organize a Society to Retain Shen Honglie 53

Resolved to Telegraph Beijing and Ping to Retain Him

Appointed Representatives to Visit Shen and Request Him Not to Resign

Qingdao Correspondence: Because Shen Honglie telegraphed Beijing to resign, various groups in Qingdao specially formed the "Qingdao Various Circles Joint Society to Retain Mayor Shen." The society held a general meeting at the Qingdao YMCA on Zhejiang Road at 2 pm today (3rd). Many representatives from various circles attended. Guo Jinnan served as chairman and reported the reasons for the meeting, saying that since Mayor Shen took office, he has done a lot for local construction, and the people have benefited from it. This time, he resigned due to the naval incident, and various groups have telegraphed the authorities, begging them to comfort and retain him. Although the central government has telegraphed to comfort and retain him, Mayor Shen has not yet dispelled his intention to resign. In order to concentrate our efforts, we have established this society. In the future, we hope that all circles will work together to achieve the goal of retaining Mayor Shen. After the report was finished, the method of retaining him was discussed: ㈠ Telegraph the authorities in Beijing and Ping to comfort and retain him. ㈡ Appoint representatives to visit Mayor Shen at 9 am tomorrow (4th) to plead with him to dispel his intention to resign. ㈢ Print and declare the intention to retain Mayor Shen to make it known to the public. This retention of Mayor Shen is purely driven by conscience and is by no means an ordinary social event. ㈣ Unite various groups and schools to go to the municipal government to retain him on a large scale. Finally, it was decided to send representatives to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Lawyers Association to ask them to join the society in order to strengthen its strength. Then, the meeting was adjourned. (July 3rd)

Antiques Discovered in Shou County 54

Many Bells, Tripods, and Cauldrons Excavated from Ancient Tombs

According to Legend, They Are Artifacts of the Spring and Autumn Period

Bengbu Correspondence: Shou County in northern Anhui Province was Shouzhou in the Qing Dynasty. In ancient times, it was called Huainan. In the Spring and Autumn Period, it was the land of Wu, Chu, Chen, and Cai. In the Warring States Period, it was merged into Chu. There are many ancient sites in the area. Recently, a large number of antiques have been discovered. According to a person from the county, there is a tall ancient tomb near Zhujiaji in the east of the county. It is said to be the tomb of the King of Chu in the Spring and Autumn Period, but it is impossible to verify which king of Chu is buried in it. It is commonly known as the Lijia Dagu Dui. Zhu Hongchu, a gentleman from Zhuji, recently saw that precious antiques were often found in the excavation of ancient tombs everywhere, so he gathered more than 150 nearby farmers and went to excavate. At that time, many antiques were dug out, including more than a dozen pairs of ancient tripods, each weighing about 100 jin. There are seal characters on the tripods. Because they have been in the soil for a long time, the handwriting is blurred, but only the two characters "Chu Yu" can be identified. They are antique and are indeed artifacts of the Spring and Autumn Period. In addition, many bronze bells and bronze cauldrons were also excavated, totaling about 7,000 jin. There are also hundreds of ancient objects of gold, silver, jade, and emerald, which are of great value. However, Zhu Hongchu kept it strictly secret from the outside world. Except for the heavy bronze utensils that are not easy to collect and can be viewed by people, other precious items are strictly stored and not allowed to be appreciated by others. Recently, it was heard that eight pieces of scattered antiques were sold, earning more than 3,000 yuan. Before long, the administrative inspector of the fourth district of Anhui Province in Shou County learned of the matter. He believed that local antiques were related to culture and should be preserved in every possible way. He sent personnel to prohibit further excavation and detained the Bao of Zhuji to strictly investigate the excavated antiques. A part of them has now been found and transported back in an attempt to preserve the ancient culture. (July 5th)

Jiading

Commissioner Requests Repair of Baoshan Embankment 55

Xu Weizhen, the administrative inspector of the sixth district, believed that the Baoshan County embankment was extremely important. He rushed to inspect it the other day. In various sections such as Zhangjiazhai, Xuejiatan, and Shidong Yanchi North Head, either the embankment foot was scoured by water and found gaps, or the embankment body was tilted outward and was about to collapse. The old embankment of Gujiadun also has a gap of about 280 feet long, which is extremely dangerous. In the event of an accident, the three counties of Tai, Jia, and Bao in the sixth district will bear the brunt. Now that the autumn flood season is approaching, it is difficult to delay any further. It is estimated that the project is about 1,380 meters long and requires about 120,000 yuan, which cannot be raised by local financial resources. He specifically returned to the office to request the provincial government to approve the rapid allocation of special funds so that they can be rushed to repair it to avoid danger.

Suzhou

Prohibition of Cattle Grazing on Graves Leads to Murder Case 58

Shen Yuan, the former chief of the Lumou Township District and a lawyer, had an ancestral tomb in Kouzhuangji. A few days ago, Wu Zihan, a man from Jiangyin, led a cow to graze on Shen's grave. Tang Genbao and others in the township told him that he could not trample on the grave to graze. Wu did not listen, which led to a fight with Tang Genbao and others. However, Wu was so powerful that Tang and others could not resist, so they gathered dozens of people from the township, each armed with weapons, and beat Wu. Wu could not resist alone, and was hit in the key point and seriously injured and fell to the ground. People carried Wu to the Gospel Hospital for treatment, but he died. The District Procuratorate sent personnel to verify it and detained Tang Genfu and his son, the ringleaders, and sent them to the court to await trial.

Wuxi

Partial Labor Strike in the Shenxin Yarn Factory 59

There are 1,550 looms and more than 700 weaving workers in the weaving room of the Shenxin No. 3 Yarn Factory in Taibaodun, outside the west gate of this county. They work 15 hours a day from 4 am to 8 pm, and can produce more than 2,000 bolts of cloth. After the January 28th Incident last year, the boycott of Japanese goods made domestic yarn and cloth strong, so the business was very prosperous. Recently, due to the coldness of resisting goods and the sluggish sales of domestic yarn and cloth, the factory implemented a reduction of two cents in wages per bolt. The female workers expressed dissatisfaction, so they asked Chen Arong, the executive director of the union, to negotiate with the factory, and agreed to reply at 10 am yesterday. However, there was no concrete solution until 11 am. More than 700 female workers suddenly went on strike. Later, Xue Mingjian, the general manager of the factory, went to the union to mediate. As a result, the wages were reduced by eight li per bolt. The female workers were satisfied and resumed work this morning (6th).

Good News for the Future of the Silk Industry 60

The spring cocoons in our county this year have been excellent due to suitable weather and good seed quality, so the harvest is extremely good. In addition, the price of silk has gradually increased. The silk farmers are happy, and the silk merchants are also looking forward to the reversal of fortunes. According to a gentleman from the silk factory industry, the price of Japanese silk has recently risen, opening at 1,000 yen. Compared with the Japanese silk five days ago, it has risen by 30 yen, and the stomach of the United States and France is very smooth. The summer silkworms of this year have now opened their leaves for the third sleep, and the number of breeding households is greater than last year. The silkworms are developing healthily. Although there will be no formal summer cocoon market for weighing and buying, there are still general cocoon makers who search for them. Recently, the shops selling autumn silkworm seeds along the road are no less than in spring. The interest of general breeding households is very strong, and there is a situation where they are too busy to respond to those who go to book in advance and buy in person. It is really a good phenomenon for the future of the silk industry.

Rice Prices Gradually Decline, Increasing Discount Rate 61

The rice industry in Xiyi has always been sold on behalf of customers. The usual practice is one cent discount per yuan, called Jiu Jiu Dui, which is common in Jing and Shanghai. Recently, due to the decline in grain prices, the discount income has been sharply reduced, which has greatly affected the expenses of various industries. After discussion by the industry, it was decided to change the old rules. The Jiu Jiu Dui will be changed to Jiu Ba Si from July 1. After the decision, a notice will be issued to the various industries, but the rice shops in various sections are deeply concerned that the increase in discounts will affect customers, so they have not been able to agree.

Local News

Wang Mingfu, Member of the Siamese Chinese Chamber of Commerce, Returns to China to Collect Goods 69

Overseas Chinese Love the Country and Promote the Sale of Domestic Goods

Wang Mingfu, the executive committee member of the Siamese Chinese Chamber of Commerce, has lived in Siam for more than 20 years. He is well respected by the local overseas Chinese and the Siamese government for his business operations. He has spared no effort in promoting domestic goods overseas. Recently, in view of the increasing number of domestic products, many of them have not yet reached Siam and are unknown, he specially returned to China from Siam to contact domestic product merchants and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce in this city in order to widely introduce them. The reporter of the New Voice Society met Wang at his hotel yesterday and talked about the following points:

Recent Situation of Overseas Chinese in Siam 70

According to Wang, there are as many as 2 million overseas Chinese in Siam, most of whom are from Guangdong Province, followed by Fujian and Zhejiang Provinces. Most of them are engaged in business in Siam. Almost all the shops in Siam are set up by our Chinese. Those who work include sawmills and rice mills. A considerable number of them are also engaged in agriculture, cultivating fields and planting crops. Therefore, in terms of financial status, our overseas Chinese contribute to the prosperity of the market and occupy an extremely important position. Although the Siamese government occasionally has various restrictions on overseas Chinese, there is still no sign of disharmony. Because our country has no commercial officers and consuls there, all important events are presided over by the General Chamber of Commerce. The solidarity of the overseas Chinese in Siam is still good, but unfortunately they all focus on the combination of fellow villagers and clans, and have not yet fully achieved the goal of overall unity.

Siamese-Chinese Trade Situation 71

In Siamese-Chinese trade, Siam's trade with China is limited to rice and wood, because the country's major products are only these two items. Therefore, only these two items are transported to our country. Most of the rice imported into our country is in the southwestern provinces, while wood is more common. According to statistics, the total amount reaches about 20 million yuan each year. Because of its tropical location, the major items that our country transports to Siam for sale are clothing materials such as silk and summer cloth. Secondly, because our overseas Chinese account for more than two-thirds of the population there, all kinds of miscellaneous items are in very considerable amounts each year due to the patriotic spirit. Now, since the Siamese Chinese Chamber of Commerce has established a domestic product exhibition hall in Siam to widely introduce them, overseas compatriots are happy to use domestic goods, so domestic goods have a very large sales market in Siam. Among the businesses of other countries in Siam, the United Kingdom and Denmark are the most prominent, but they are mostly engaged in machinery businesses. However, in recent years, Japanese goods have gradually filled the market. Coupled with the impact of the world economic depression, the business situation of our overseas Chinese has also been affected.

Education of Overseas Chinese Children 72

As for the education of overseas Chinese children,

There are about 100 elementary schools established by themselves, which are still common. There is only one junior high school, Xinmin. Now we plan to set up a high school, with a budget of more than 20,000 yuan, but the amount is relatively large, and the preparation is a little difficult, so it is still in the planning stage. However, since April of this year, the Siamese government has ordered each school to teach Siamese history and geography for more than 20 hours a week. After negotiations with the Siamese government by the Chamber of Commerce, the government agreed to reduce the time, but it has not been completely resolved.

Return to China to Collect Goods 73

I came to Shanghai this time because the Chinese Chamber of Commerce is building a large auditorium, completely modeled after our country's modern architectural style, and it is expected to be completed around Double Ten Festival. Inside the auditorium, domestic products are displayed all around for wide introduction, so I was specially commissioned to come to Shanghai to solicit samples from various manufacturers. Now, after contacting the product exhibition hall in this city, there have been considerable results. I will stay in Shanghai for about two weeks. Once the collection of domestic product samples is completed, I will return to Siam to arrange them, and so on.

South China Typhoon Causes Heavy Losses to Ships 77

Cargo Washed Away by Huge Waves

In the past three days, a typhoon occurred in the South China Sea, causing varying degrees of damage to commercial ships sailing in the area. Yesterday, this city received telegrams from Shantou and Xiamen reporting that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Tonghua" steamer, which was on its way from Shanghai to Xiamen, encountered the typhoon when it was about to reach the waters outside Xiamen port. The strength of the typhoon, the height of the raging waves, and the intensity of the wind and waves were rare. Fortunately, the "Tonghua" took precautions in advance and anchored to avoid the wind. Twenty large barrels of raw oil stored on the upper deck of the ship were washed away by a huge wave. The wave crashed through the ship, and the twenty barrels of oil were completely washed into the sea and sank to the bottom. In addition, more than a hundred pieces of deck cargo were also partially washed into the sea, and the other part was soaked by the waves, resulting in enormous losses. Fortunately, the ship was able to maintain its position with the help of huge anchors; otherwise, it would have been in danger. The "Yuanda" steamer in the waters off Xiamen also suffered the same danger. More than sixty pieces of deck cargo were soaked and heavily damaged by the typhoon and huge waves. Currently, the Hakka people in Xiamen require the shipowner to be responsible for the cargo washed away by the sea waves. They must report to the customs and obtain proof of the cargo being lost at sea before they can claim compensation from the insurance company. Several other commercial ships have suffered similar damage.

It is reported that several fishing boats at sea have been sunk by the typhoon, and an investigation is currently underway.

Shanghai Power Company Statement 78

The Company Serves the Public

Workers Serve the Company

Those Who Obstruct Must Be Dismissed

A labor dispute has occurred at the Shanghai Power Company, as reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday, the company issued a statement saying that the cause of the dispute was that a worker claimed to have been dismissed without receiving compensation. After a thorough investigation by the company's Chinese and foreign staff, it was found that the worker had resigned voluntarily after being reprimanded for a work error. Senior staff members tried to persuade him to return to work, but he insisted on resigning. According to the company's regulations, dismissed employees, except those who were dismissed for misconduct, are given compensation based on the length of their service. However, those who resign voluntarily are not given compensation unless they have served for more than twenty years. The worker in question had only worked for the company for three and a half years and was not entitled to compensation according to the regulations. Therefore, he lied to his colleagues that he had been dismissed in order to obtain the compensation. Other employees believed this lie and, without consulting the company, held a meeting in the factory yard during working hours, causing disturbances. This type of action is sufficient to hinder the company's service to the public. The company, in view of the importance of serving the public, issued a notice to its employees in accordance with the principles of managing public utilities, stating: "1. This company is responsible for continuously supplying electricity and cannot allow interruptions in electricity supply unless factories are shut down, causing thousands of workers to lose their jobs. This Monday afternoon, some workers suddenly refused to work without prior notice and caused disturbances without consulting the company, thus hindering the company's service. This company has repeatedly stated that it is willing to discuss any reasonable issues with its colleagues. However, without first consulting the company or considering the company's responsibility to the public, they rashly caused disturbances. This company cannot tolerate employees stopping their service to the public for selfish purposes through strikes or other means. No one is allowed to stop working, gather for meetings, or cause disturbances during working hours that obstruct the company's service. In order to protect the company's service to the public, anyone who causes disturbances, stops working, gathers for meetings, or uses other methods to obstruct the company's business during working hours will be dismissed. This company always has extra staff ready to ensure the company's service to the public and the uninterrupted supply of electricity. All loyal colleagues who are willing to work as usual will be given thorough protection." Unfortunately, some employees, without first consulting the company or considering their responsibility to the public, have already caused disturbances in an attempt to obstruct the company's service to the public. The company is therefore taking the position that it will not allow any interruption in electricity supply, given the importance of this service. The company usually provides its workers with special treatment because it recognizes that public utilities have a responsibility to provide continuous service. However, in the event of a strike, those who disregard their responsibility to the public and obstruct the service of public utilities have already automatically terminated their right to serve the public. Therefore, the company cannot negotiate with them.

Safety Association 80

Rubber Guild 81

Singapore's New Import Goods Falsification Penalties 85

Consul in Penang Asks Chinese Exporters to Pay Attention

Exporters in this city, for the sake of small profits, often combine various small items into large items when transporting goods to Penang and Singapore, and use vacuum tubes as empty bottles. The packaging does not indicate that the Straits Transport Alliance, after discovering this malpractice, appointed an inspection committee stationed in Singapore, authorized to inspect. Once discovered, the penalties are doubled. The Consulate in Penang reported the above situation to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which forwarded it to the Ministry of Industry, which forwarded it to the International Trade Bureau of this city for verification and handling. After receiving the order, the Bureau has separately sent letters to the City Chamber of Commerce and exporters, reminding them to pay attention. The instructions of the Ministry of Industry and the report of the Consulate in Penang are extracted and recorded below.

Ministry of Industry Instructions 86

The International Trade Bureau received the Ministry of Industry's Commerce Character No. 18520 instructions yesterday, stating: "For compliance purposes, enclosed is a report from the Consulate in Penang dated May 1st of the 22nd year, regarding the filling in of packaging by exporters, which can be used as a reference. A copy of the original text is enclosed for your inspection." After review by the Ministry, it is deemed that the matter concerns the interests of exporters. A copy of the original text is enclosed, ordering the Bureau to immediately comply, and to inform exporters in various places that they must not falsify the filling in of packaging in the future, so as to avoid being discovered, penalized, and suffering losses. This order.

Consulate Report 87

The Consulate in Penang reported on May 1st regarding the filling in of packaging that exporters should pay attention to, stating: "Merchants in various places often falsify things when transporting goods to Singapore and other ports in the Far East in order to save freight. The words written on the packaging of the goods are written incorrectly, so that they are different from the contents. In order to rectify freight revenue, the Straits Transport Alliance appointed a goods inspection committee, stationed in Singapore, authorized to the inspector to check the contents of the goods shipped to the port from other places in front of the receiving personnel at any time to see if the contents of the goods are consistent with what is stated on the outside of the packaging. It is said that many goods shipped to Singapore, small items are combined with large items, and only the name of the large item is written on the packaging. Sometimes a batch of vacuum tubes is marked as empty bottles, their value is very different, and the freight can be reduced. It is found that this is an act of collusion between the exporter and the consignee, not a careless mistake on the packaging at one time. This kind of falsification has been around for a long time, but the Straits Transport Alliance only recently discovered it. In order to rectify revenue, there is now a method of appointing an inspector."

Additional Penalties 88

And additional penalties are added, in order to warn those who profit from this. The inspection method started with the Dutch East Indies Transportation Authority in the Dutch East Indies, which first formulated the same inspection method. The Straits Settlements, China, Japan and other places have followed their method to formulate regulations and formally implement them. When each cargo is found by the inspector to be inconsistent with what is marked, and the freight of what is marked is lower than the freight of the cargo, then the freight should be fined one time, and the importer is ordered to pay the real freight, the difference between the original marked freight and the difference, and the fine, before the goods can be picked up. According to the investigation, the Transportation Alliance will decide

The method was sent to Singapore, and the board of directors of the Western Chamber of Commerce also held a meeting to discuss it, and believed that the matter was feasible, and decided to forward this method to all for their information. It is said that the general honest importers welcomed this inspection step, but there are also those who, although they have never falsified, have skeptical opinions about this method, because they believe that the goods shipped to Singapore will be opened, and they are very reluctant, and when they are not opened, they will try to find a way to avoid being inspected, but they will not succeed. After being angry, they immediately raised an objection, and then the Transportation Alliance authorities and the inspectors explained the various situations in detail, and then cancelled the objection, and believed that this method was indeed beneficial to careful importers. As this method has been implemented, there will be more complicated procedures for imported goods, but the Straits Transport Alliance has decided to implement it, and the Western Chamber of Commerce has also expressed its approval, and it is imperative. In the future, exporters in our country should pay extreme attention to the packaging of goods and the reporting of their contents, so as to avoid unnecessary losses.

Shanghai Telephone Company Statement Regarding Five-Cent Call Fee 89

The Shanghai Telephone Company issued a statement yesterday, saying that recent news reports about the cancellation of the five-cent Chinese-foreign call fee are one-sided. The company believes that the contract signed on April 19th stipulates that the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and the Shanghai Telephone Company charge five cents per call from the user making the call. This fee was originally set seven years ago, and although telephone fees have been increased by both parties, this fee has remained unchanged. Now the Telephone Bureau wants to cancel this fee, so that its fewer users can also benefit from the larger telephone network of the Telephone Company. On the contrary, the Telephone Company has no equal benefits. The result will be that all users in the Public Concession and the French Concession will bear the cost of calls, otherwise, according to the current method, only the person making the call will bear the cost.
