Zhabei Silk Factory Strike Affects Entire District 90

Zhengfeng and Others Resume Work Then Stop Again

Commotion Occurs During Persuasion

Social Affairs Bureau to Mediate Tomorrow

Police Suppress With Batons This Morning After Work Resumes

The Zhabei Zhengfeng and other silk factory workers went on strike in unison on the afternoon of the day before yesterday because they demanded the restoration of wages and the factory did not give a concrete reply. It has been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that after the Party and police agencies summoned representatives from the factory and workers to persuade them, the situation between the two sides has eased, and it was decided to resume work as usual starting yesterday morning. However, the Chuxin and other silk factories on Changan Road also went on strike yesterday morning, thus expanding the scope. Also, because the situation of the workers is complicated, there were even incidents of troublemaking taking advantage of the opportunity. Fortunately, the police stations in each district maintained order, so accidents were avoided. The Social Affairs Bureau has scheduled to summon representatives from both the factory and the workers tomorrow (the 8th) for mediation. The situation yesterday is recorded separately as follows:

Meeting and Resuming Work After Zhengfeng, Yichang, Yifengsheng, Yuncheng, Changfeng, Zhengda, Xiangcheng, Yongting, and other silk factory workers went on strike in unison the day before yesterday (the 5th), they still gathered together and did not disperse until around 5:50 p.m., when

The police brigade persuaded them to return home in batches, and then they dispersed. The Zhabei Fourth District Party Headquarters, the Silk Industry Union, and the Fifth District Third Branch Office immediately convened representatives from the above-mentioned factories at the Hujia Muqiao Fire Station to discuss solutions. Those present included Shen Sheng from the Fourth District Party Headquarters, Chen Xiuchang from the Labor Union, Wen Yishan, Chief of the Third Branch Office of the Fifth District, Wang Zixuan from Yichang, Wang Shenqingyi from the Branch Factory, Wei Kunjiang from Fengsheng, Yu Jingfang from Zhengfeng, Zhou Shuyin from Yuncheng, Yu Wengui from Changfeng, Cha Jianshi from Zhengda, Zhang Peikun from Xiangcheng, and Yuan Bingzhang from Yongting. At first, the representatives of each factory insisted on implementing the announcement of the stoppage of the machinery. After the Party and police persuaded them, they immediately agreed on three solutions: 1. Each factory will continue to resume work on the morning of the 6th. It does not matter how many workers come to work, or the time of arrival, whether early or late. The economy is also not considered. 2. The workers will be guided by union officials to return to work in all directions on the same evening (the 5th). There must be no more strikes or disturbances. The issue of salary increases will be resolved after waiting for the Party and government agencies. 3. Each factory will be protected by the police dispatched by each branch office to maintain order.

Stopped Again in the Afternoon After the meeting, union officials went to various factories to persuade the workers to resume work. Therefore, the factories resumed operation normally yesterday morning (the 6th). In the morning, Yichang and its two branch factories all arrived at the factory, but the time of arrival varied. Yifengsheng only had one-tenth of its workers, Zhengfeng had seven-tenths, Yuncheng had one-tenth, Changfeng had six-tenths, Zhengda had all, Xiangcheng had one-tenth, Yongting had eight-tenths, and Fulunheng did not participate in the strike, so there was no problem. By the afternoon, the workers learned that 27 other silk factories in Zhabei had gone on strike, and there would be unfavorable news for the factories that had already resumed work. Therefore, they all waited and watched. So, except for Yichang, they all stopped work again starting in the afternoon. At the same time, at around 5:50 p.m., when the Party and Yichang and its two branch factories were about to close, dozens of hooligans suddenly appeared, holding dirty things, and lingered near there, intending to demonstrate to the workers of the factory. Fortunately, the nearby police officers noticed this and immediately reported it to the police station. A large number of police officers were dispatched to suppress them, so they were able to prevent other changes from happening. However, the workers were therefore afraid, so the problem of a full resumption of work today (the 7th) is still difficult to predict. Among them, Yuncheng and Zhengfeng factories announced that they would stop work for one day today (the 7th) to repair the machinery and furnaces, which were damaged, and have reported to the Party and government agencies for the record. The workers of Xiangcheng and Yifengsheng factories are said to be able to resume work without any problems if other factories formally resume work.

Affected the Entire District There are 31 silk factories that have started work in Zhabei District 1. Since Zhengfeng and other factories went on strike, 800 male and female workers from the Fuchang silk factory on Hutai Road suddenly went on strike together at 6:00 a.m. yesterday. After the Sixth District Silk Workers' Union sent people to persuade them, they all resumed work at 10:00 a.m. In the afternoon at 1:00 p.m., the female workers of Fengtaishun in Dayang Bridge and Yutai in Tanziwan also went on strike together, and the order was chaotic. They gathered together to demand that the silk factories take unified action. As a result, 27 factories in Zhabei District Changan Road Maofeng, Qianyuan, Xiexin, Hongsheng, Chuxin, Jiyu Xieji, Zhenxing, Baotaishun, Yuanxin, Gonghe Road Jiyu Taiji, Dayang Bridge Fengtaishun, Tanziwan Yutai, Hutai Road Fuchang, Zhongxing Road Gongda, Tanjiaqiao Maoli, Dasheng Bridge Tiansheng, Gujiawan Xinglun, Guangfu Road Jiatai, Hongchun, Nanmeiyuan Road Wuxing, Hengfeng Road Meifeng, Yuanfeng, Fuyuan, Shentai, Yutong Road Yuanxing, Yuanji, Gujiawan Yufeng, and other 27 workers also went on strike one after another.

Commotion Occurred When the workers of Qianyuan and other factories went on strike, Yang Gengti, Yuan Yunlong, Wu Suzhen, and other members of the Sixth District Silk Workers' Union, led all the cadres to set off in different directions to persuade the workers. The police chief of the Fourth District General Department of the Public Security Bureau also set off to maintain order and persuade the workers. Female workers from the Chuxin Silk Factory on Changan Road refused to listen to persuasion, resulting in a conflict with the police officers. One patrolman from the Fourth District was injured by a thrown stone. Two female workers who caused the incident were arrested, and after being reprimanded by the district chief, they were released immediately because they were ignorant.

Resume Work Today 91

After the workers of various silk factories were persuaded by the Party, government, and police agencies, they expressed their acceptance. Because of various problems yesterday, they did not all work as usual. After consultation between the union and the Silk Industry Association, fearing that the workers might be incited by one or two hooligans and cause trouble everywhere, they decided to formally prepare a letter, earnestly requesting each police station to dispatch a large number of police officers to protect the workers going to work at the gates of each silk factory this morning. After receiving the letter, each district dispatched police officers overnight in batches, together with the police brigade, to maintain order.

Reasons for the Strike 92

The wages of the female factory workers were originally six corners, with four days of monthly reward and three corners of weekly reward. The wages of the male workers were calculated on a monthly basis with four days of monthly reward. Each silkworm moth was paid one dollar and four and a half corners per month. Because the price of silk fell, the wages were reduced to 70%. A strike occurred, and later it was changed to 75%. Until this year, the price of silk rose, but the employer replied that the wages of the male workers would be calculated on a monthly basis, and the monthly salary would be increased according to the performance of the silkworm moth subsidy, one dollar and two corners per person per month. Workers who worked for one month were rewarded with two days of work. The wages of the female workers were calculated on a daily basis, four corners and eight cents per person per month, and those who worked for one week were rewarded with two corners, and those who worked for one month were rewarded with two days of work. According to the Fourth District Silk Industry Union, the sudden strike of the workers in various factories was caused by the disagreement between Yongheng and Zhengfeng factories. Yongting workers went to the front of Zhengfeng factory at noon when they were off work to instigate, saying that Yongheng had already gone on strike, so that a small number of Zhengfeng workers launched it first and then affected all of them. Later, the workers of Zhengfeng saw that the workers of Yongheng were still working, so they accused them of spreading rumors and instigating, so that they also went on strike and affected various factories. Therefore, this incident was actually a labor-capital problem caused by the jealousy of the employer.

Mediation Tomorrow 93

After the Social Affairs Bureau received the joint application for mediation from the Third, Fourth, and Sixth Districts Silk Industry Union on the 3rd of this month, fearing that strikes and other things would happen, it sent Zhang Chuqiang to investigate on the 4th. After the workers in each district went on strike for several days, it also sent people to investigate thoroughly and scheduled to summon the Silk Factory Industry Association and the Silk Industry Unions of the Third, Fourth, and Sixth Districts at 10:00 a.m. tomorrow to conduct mediation. A notice was issued yesterday, stating: "For notification purposes, the case is that silk factory workers are demanding the restoration of their original treatment. This bureau has scheduled to summon you at 10:00 a.m. on the 8th of this month to conduct an interview. We hereby urgently notify the association to send two responsible representatives each to attend the bureau on time and listen to the interview. This is to notify, Director Wu Xingya."

Shanghai Telephone Bureau Cracks Down on Public Telephone Attendants' Misconduct 96

The management fees for attendants are deducted monthly from the call fees, with a minimum allowance of two yuan, a very generous arrangement. Attendants should be conscientious and dedicated to their duties. However, recent reports indicate that some attendants are secretly increasing call fees, which is tantamount to fraud and should be strictly prohibited. In addition to dispatching undercover investigators, we hereby inform you that you must strictly adhere to the prescribed call fees and collect them accurately. Any private charges or additional fees will result in immediate disconnection and heavy fines. Please do not make a mistake."

China National Industries Federation Publishes Yan Qingxiang's Account of Meeting with the Italian Prime Minister 98

The New Sound News Agency reports that Yan Qingxiang, the employer representative attending the International Labour Conference, sent a letter from Rome to the China National Industries Federation, detailing his visit with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. "I was ordered to attend the International Labour Conference, embarking on the 10th of April and setting sail the next day. I arrived in Venice, Italy, on May 5th and went to Rome the following day. Our ambassador to Italy was originally to be Kong Xiangxi, but since Kong had not yet taken office, the eldest son of the former ambassador to Japan, Wang Rongbao, was acting as chargé d'affaires. After briefly resting, I went to the embassy to meet with Wang and Consul Zhu. After a brief exchange, Consul Zhu accompanied me to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Labour and Capital, the Central Party Headquarters, and the General Labour Union for courtesy visits, where I was received with sincerity. Wang, as chargé d'affaires, negotiated with the Italian Ministry of Foreign Affairs for my audience with Prime Minister Mussolini, scheduled for 6:00 PM on May 12th at the Prime Minister's office in the State Council. Wang accompanied me from my residence to the State Council. Upon arriving at the State Council, an adjutant led me to the waiting room. Because the Prime Minister was already receiving a guest, I waited for about half an hour. The adjutant then announced the Prime Minister's order to invite the guest in. Wang and I arrived at the Prime Minister's office, and the guards opened the door. As soon as I stepped inside, I found the room unusually dark, with only a single electric light in the corner, its light dim and indistinct. The room was very large, about seventy feet wide and one hundred forty feet deep. In the center of the room were two large writing desks, three large chairs, and nothing else. After walking a few steps, my eyes suddenly flashed with light, as if a famous actor had taken the stage, with the curtains drawn open. Despite the size of the room, the simple furnishings gave it an empty, unadorned feel. The sudden flash of light was startling, and few people would not be surprised and lose their composure. I am normally insensitive, but I felt undisturbed and calm, even more so than usual, and continued to move forward with purpose. Mussolini had already risen from his seat to greet me. He was wearing an army uniform, tall and imposing, but his appearance was very gentle. After Wang introduced me, we shook hands. Mussolini first said that he was very sorry for keeping me waiting because of the previous guest. He then asked us to sit down, and he leaned on the writing desk with both hands and talked to us. After paying my respects, I began to discuss administrative and party affairs, organizational structures, and industrial conditions, which he explained in great detail. Before leaving, he presented me with two signed photographs, with the words 'Sincere Respect' inscribed on them. Wang told me that Mussolini rarely did this and that his treatment of me was exceptional. I thanked him and stood up to say goodbye. Mussolini firmly shook my hand, patted my back, and escorted me to the door, saying, 'I apologize for not being able to entertain you more during your stay in our capital.' I bowed and thanked him again, and we shook hands before parting. As we left, Wang told me that Mussolini usually did not smile and that his demeanor was often stern when meeting with guests. His change in demeanor today, showing such kindness to you, is a testament to the respect foreign politicians have for industrialists. Even high-ranking political and military officials from our country have not been able to win his favor, making one feel inferior." Since meeting with Prime Minister Mussolini, I have had many observations during my stay here. In summary, I would say that "the intelligence of the Italian people is not as great as that of the Chinese, but their faith is stronger." Thus, a man of his generation, such as Mussolini, has been able to take advantage of the times, reform politics, encourage agriculture and industry, and turn Italy into a first-class power in ten years. He is now taking further steps to organize large-scale industrial alliances, such as the rayon manufacturers, who are forming a joint company to reduce domestic competition and concentrate their efforts externally. This is just one example. Looking back at our country's industries, which lack communication and unity, resembling a heap of loose sand, and where jealousy among peers is deeply ingrained and difficult to break, how can we hope for a day of revitalization? I sincerely hope that domestic industrialists can quickly begin to cooperate and organize themselves to avoid being eliminated and defeated one by one in the future. Regarding the fact that the Italian party does not interfere in politics and the regulations that prevent it from doing so, I admire Mussolini's great courage and means. The city party headquarters' budget and final accounts must be submitted to the mayor for approval before being forwarded to the provincial party headquarters and then to the central party headquarters. All people's organizations, those belonging to the city are controlled by the mayor, those belonging to the province are controlled by the provincial governor, and those belonging to the whole country are controlled by the Minister of Labour and Capital. Mussolini started from the party but is not bound by it. This kind of courage and means is unique to Mussolini in the world. Therefore, I have repeatedly thought about how to make our country like Italy today. But it depends on people. If the important figures who now hold the central power can make good use of their opportunities to guide and protect the people, putting the people first in everything and strengthening the people's faith, and if the people can also understand the government's difficulties in doing things and not make unwarranted demands, realizing spiritual unity, then perhaps China's new life will begin at this moment. Otherwise, with foreign troubles unresolved and internal strife arising again, and people's livelihoods deteriorating, great disasters are coming. The root of national subjugation lies in poverty and weakness. Therefore, if we want to turn poverty into wealth and weakness into strength today, it is essential to completely reorganize the entire industry and commerce of the country, and especially to have a complete united organization. Are there any of my intelligent compatriots and the current industrial leaders who believe in my words and sympathize with me? Then this article is not in vain."

German Merchants Suffer Losses of Over One Million

Japanese Merchants Seek to Take Advantage of the Opportunity

The New Sound News Agency reports that since the National Socialist Party, led by Hitler, came to power in Germany, an extreme anti-Jewish movement has prevailed. This has aroused resentment among Jewish financiers around the world, who wield tremendous financial power, towards the German dictatorial regime. Jews in Britain and France have launched boycotts of German goods as economic resistance and retaliation. The New Sound News Agency reporter investigated this deteriorating situation towards Germany yesterday, which has recently spread to Shanghai. According to foreign sources, Jews residing in Shanghai have long harboured resentment towards German expatriates and have been brewing a boycott movement against Germany for three months. Not only are they generally rejecting German goods, but they have also successively broken trade contracts with major commercial institutions such as German shipping and insurance companies. It is estimated that the German side has suffered losses of over one million yuan. The anti-German attitude of Jewish capitalists in Shanghai, such as Sassoon and Kadoorie, has attracted much attention. It is also reported that after the Jews launched the anti-German goods movement, they immediately engaged in secret negotiations with the commercial authorities of the British, French, Italian, and Japanese consulates, seeking to establish trade relations with those countries to eliminate relations with Germany. The Japanese commercial authorities and business community in Shanghai are actively negotiating with the Jews with certain conditions in order to expand Japanese economic power in Shanghai.

Land Value Tax Collection Cannot be Implemented This Year 103

The Central News Agency reports that regarding the collection of land value tax in the Shanghai city area, the reporter interviewed Jin Liren, Director of the Land Bureau, yesterday. According to him, the collection of land value tax will not be implemented this year due to complicated procedures. It is not true that the collection will begin in July. The Legislative Yuan has not yet approved the "Shanghai City Land Value Tax Collection Measures." Although it was submitted to the central government for approval, no reply has been received yet. Even if the Executive Yuan promulgates the revised regulations for collecting land value tax, it is still necessary to carry out investigation and valuation procedures. Therefore, the date of collection cannot be determined. Land in this city has only been subject to land tax, paying only one yuan and five cents per mu, which is unfair. This city is a major commercial port, and land prices are not uniform. The price of each mu may be worth hundreds, thousands, or even hundreds of thousands. Now, land value tax is collected as a percentage. The Valuation Committee will assess the land prices in various places and then determine the tax amount according to the regulations. If a landowner believes it is inappropriate, they can request a change at any time, but the final decision rests with the government. This method is based on the Premier's land policy. Since this city's situation is different from other provinces and cities, handling land value tax can enrich the city treasury to develop municipal facilities. If it can be handled smoothly, it will truly realize the Premier's aim of equalizing land rights.

Revenue from Passenger and Freight Transport on the Two Railways in the First Half of This Year 104

Totaled Over Nine Million Yuan

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus announced that the revenue from passenger and freight transport on the two railways in the first half of the 22nd year amounted to 9,043,597.95 yuan. The Shanghai-Nanjing line accounted for 5,886,118.49 yuan, approximately 65.1% of the total. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line accounted for 3,157,479.46 yuan, approximately 34.9% of the total. The revenue from passenger transport on the two railways totaled 6,869,309.32 yuan, approximately 75.9% of the total. The revenue from freight transport totaled 2,174,288.63 yuan, approximately 24.1% of the total. Comparing passenger and freight transport on the two railways from January to May, freight transport accounted for a maximum of 25.2%. In June, freight transport increased, accounting for approximately 31.6%.

The first joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees of the two industries was originally scheduled to be convened on August 10th. Now, in order to plan and address the situation, the meeting is specially advanced to 3:00 PM on the 10th of this month at this association (427 Fumin Road, Dananmen, Nanshi). In addition to sending a separate circular, we hereby send this special letter to you. We urge you to examine this matter and attend the meeting on time. If you are unable to attend due to unforeseen circumstances, you should immediately entrust a representative familiar with the history of the tobacco and alcohol industries with official authorization and notify this association in advance in order to comply with the law and facilitate the association's work. This matter concerns the interests of the two industries, so please do not ignore or abandon it. The Joint Association of the Shanghai, Nanjing, and Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industries, signed by Chen Liangyu, Chairman; Yu Xunlu, Standing Committee Member; Zhang Suhou, Shen Weiting, Cao Gexian, Chairman; Zhang Dalian, Standing Committee Member; Jin Yunjie, Jin Jiayue, Dai Zhuoan, and Chen Weiwen."

The Bicycle Association Sends a Letter Requesting Protection for Bicycles 113

Regarding the Detention of Bicycles for No Reason

The Shanghai Bicycle Repair and Rental Association sent a letter yesterday to the Municipal Government bureaus, the Chinese Ratepayers Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and other organizations regarding the Western police detaining bicycles: "We are writing to inform you that we recently received a petition from dozens of our members in the Xinzha District, including Xin Tongxing, complaining about the Western police in the Xinzha Police Station detaining bicycles for no reason. We have already submitted a petition requesting that measures be taken to stop this, and we were informed that the matter had been forwarded to higher authorities for negotiation and prevention. However, the Western police have now intensified their actions, urging Chinese police officers in various streets to order any bicycles passing by to stop and carry out detentions. The police station is imposing excessive fines, detaining people, and impounding vehicles, engaging in all kinds of insults. Even cyclists with their own bicycles are fined 50 cents, while those renting bicycles are fined 3 yuan. These vehicles have not violated any regulations, and some vehicles were detained just after being pushed out of the shop and before anyone had even gotten on them. Since this happened, the losses suffered by the merchants have been significant. Under these circumstances, who would dare to rent or ride a bicycle? What will become of our industry? We have been operating this business for many years, paying taxes and complying with the Public Works Department's regulations. We are legitimate merchants who should be protected by the police, not arbitrarily destroyed. Moreover, the bicycle originated in Europe and the United States and is now popular in our country. Because it is lightweight and economical, everyone cherishes it. In places where roads have not been built, it can be relied upon to facilitate transportation. Now, under the entire legal system of the Public Works Department, this same unfortunate event does not occur in other police districts, but only in the Xinzha District. If we do not request immediate measures to stop this, our livelihood will be cut off.' Based on this, our association has specially sent responsible representatives Li Xiaoshi, Xu Zhongliang, Chen Langen, and Sun Hongchun to present the hardships to you. We respectfully request that you promptly negotiate with the Police Department of the Public Works Department to alleviate the merchants' difficulties and maintain their business."

The New Drug Association Issues a Statement on Epidemic Prevention Medicines 114

Paying Attention to Cheaply Marketed Products

The New Drug Association has repeatedly received reports from various circles stating that various newly emerged epidemic prevention waters on the market are numerous, but their prices are surprisingly low. Not only are they ineffective, but they can even cause death. Deceiving oneself and others is going too far. How can the association, as the collective organization of the new drug industry, not inquire about these harmful drugs? Because the matter concerns social public health, the association issued the following statement after a meeting yesterday: "Epidemic prevention water is an essential medicine for summer emergencies. Not only must the ingredients be specially authentic, but the manufacturing process must also be extremely careful to achieve good results. The member pharmacies of this association hold business licenses approved by the Health Bureau, employ pharmacists registered with the Ministry of Health, and act carefully in accordance with medical principles. Therefore, their products can be guaranteed to be free of the above-mentioned malpractices. Although the cost is high, because it is related to emergency care, we are unwilling to raise prices to make excessive profits, nor do we engage in price-cutting sales. We sincerely hope that all circles will pay attention to this and consider it fortunate."

Renowned Physician Wu Guanying Receives Special Award from the University of Paris, France 115

Renowned Physician Mr. Wu Guanying graduated from the Aurora University School of Medicine in Shanghai in the autumn of the 16th year of the Republic of China. He subsequently received a public grant from the university to further his studies in France, specializing in internal medicine. In 1931, he graduated from the doctoral program at the University of Paris. His dissertation was on the phenomenon of excitement of diabetic patients after being stimulated by blood sugar. After evaluation by professors and members of the medical research institute of the university, it was considered to be a valuable academic work, and he was awarded a silver medal by the university. In France, this silver medal is not easily obtained even by French people unless they have special academic knowledge. Mr. Wu is said to be the first Chinese student in France to receive this award. It is reported that Mr. Wu has now returned to China and has been hired by the Peking Central Hospital as the chief physician.

Unemployed and Heartbroken Young Man Attempts Suicide in Library 116

Fortunately, He Was Rescued After Taking Only a Small Dose of Poison

A Suicide Note Expressing Extreme Sadness and Despair

Eyes Weeping Blood, Heart Turned to Ashes, Unbearable Memories

Yesterday at around 10:00 AM, in the Shanghai Shenbao Circulation Library on the third floor of the Er Ma Lu Continental Emporium, a young man came to the reading room to browse newspapers and books. The young man was wearing a white twill cloth shirt, white serge pants, and yellow leather shoes. At 11:15 AM, the young man suddenly

Turned Pale 117

and collapsed to the ground. When discovered by the library staff member Mr. Gu, he thought it was a case of acute痧症 (acute illness) and immediately stepped forward to help him up. Unexpectedly, he was already on the verge of death, vomiting white foam from his mouth non-stop, and unable to speak. Seeing this, Mr. Gu immediately reported the situation to the concession ambulance and the Central Police Station by telephone. Before the police arrived, a note was found on the reading table, which read, "I really don't have the strength to go to Wusong to drown myself, so please forgive me for dying here." Followed by the words "Weakling Le Shang", "same day" etc. After this note was discovered, it was known that the young man had

Attempted Suicide by Poisoning 118

A paper package was also found beside him, containing several letters, as well as short pants, a fountain pen, a handkerchief, and a suicide note addressed to his lover and a few words written on the eve of the suicide, which are transcribed below. After a while, Police Officer No. 287 and an ambulance arrived. They immediately took the young man to Renji Hospital for treatment. His Consciousness Returned 119

and he was out of danger. When asked why he attempted suicide, he resolutely refused to reveal the truth. Judging from the letters he wrote before his suicide, it can be inferred that Jin Mogeng is now unemployed and has a lover (referred to as Hong in the letters) who abandoned him due to his unemployment, leading to loneliness and unhappiness. He felt that life was meaningless, so he developed a pessimistic view of the world and attempted suicide by taking poison yesterday morning. The suicide note to his lover and a new-style poem, as well as a few words written before the suicide, are transcribed below:

Letter to Lover 120

(1) Hong, I don't hate you, nor do I hate your current lover, Jin. In short, in this whole society filled with the stench of money, pure love can never exist. What is called love in today's society is just a term for the mutual self-deception of both parties based on emotional or carnal impulses and mutual needs. You must know that in an unreasonable society, there is unreasonable married life. I am a high-spirited man who has wasted his time until now, stubborn as ever, and of course, I must bravely struggle forward. However, this letter was originally intended to be a complete and systematic text, but looking back on the past, it is unbearable to recall. My eyes are weeping blood, my heart is turned to ashes. My heart wants to write, but my strength is not enough, so I have to put down my pen, forever put down my pen. July 3, 1933. (2) Hong, you are unfaithful, you are truly unfaithful, you have let me down until now. I remember when we sang softly and talked intimately, one word was worth a thousand gold. Words Before Suicide 121

(A few words on the eve of suicide) I am unwilling to flatter and fawn, nor am I capable of cleverly seizing and plundering. In this deformed society, it is natural that I cannot find a job, and it is natural that I am looked down upon and ridiculed. The pressure I have suffered in life is already extremely unbearable, and at the same time, my companion who has been my only comfort in the past three years of mutual dependence...

Bail Canceled for Soviet Assistance Association Staff Member 122

Police Declare Withdrawal of Appeal

Alexander Morrison, a Russian national and the director of the chemical supplies department of the Soviet Assistance Association at No. 2 Beijing Road, was recently criticized by the Soviet authorities for not diligently carrying out the political work assigned to him in China by the Soviet Defense Political Bureau. Therefore, Markov was selected to come to China to take over the political work from Morrison. After Markov arrived in Shanghai, he organized an active working committee, with Morrison as one of the members, to carry out the work. However, Morrison was under heavy surveillance everywhere, which prevented him from proceeding, and his opinions differed from Markov's. There was a plan to send Morrison back to Moscow. Morrison, fearing that he would be executed like several others who had been sent back to Russia, abandoned his post and fled to Hankou to avoid the situation. Markov, fearing that Morrison would leak secrets, accused Morrison of embezzling 25,000 silver dollars. Morrison, upon hearing the news, rushed back to Shanghai and surrendered himself. After investigation by the First Special District Court, he was found not guilty. The police declared an appeal, and Morrison was ordered to post bail. This matter has been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, the police lawyer, Ru Bao-yi, declared the withdrawal of the appeal to the First Special District Court's Criminal Division 1. Judge Qian, since the police did not appeal, ordered the cancellation of Morrison's bail.

Record of Meeting of the Gao An Snow Vindication Committee of the Barber Industry 128

The Shanghai Barber Industry Gao An Snow Vindication Committee held its 14th executive committee meeting at the Nan Shi Xie Qiao Barber Association yesterday morning at 11:00 AM. Committee members Xue Guangdian, Guan Zhihe, Luo Shantao, Pan Zhenshan, Zhang Yujin, Qian Shouling, Wang Changxing, Chen Youshou, and 19 other committee members attended the meeting. Gao Yuanlin, the father of the deceased, and Hu Shunyuan, representing Guo Wanhai, were also present. The standing committee member Chen Sijiang was elected as the chairman. After the formalities were completed, the chairman first reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that since the Gao case occurred,

it has been two months, and negotiations have been hopeless. The anger of the industry is extraordinary. If this continues, the matter will inevitably end without resolution. However, for the sake of our own interests, we, the industry, must seek a final solution to comfort the deceased's soul and uphold justice. Next, various committee members spoke one after another to discuss the progress of negotiations on the Gao case. It was decided to hold the second industry congress on a fixed date and submit a large petition to various agencies at the same time after the congress. All members unanimously approved the decision. Next, the method of convening the congress was discussed. Because many members of the industry in the North and South Municipal Concessions are concerned about overcrowding the venue when meetings are held on the same day, it was decided to convene meetings in separate districts over four days. The date of the meeting will be July 17 for members of the French Concession, July 18 for members of the British Concession, July 19 for members of the Nan Shi, July 20 for members of the Zhabei, and July 21 for the general congress of representatives of the city's industry. At the same time, a large petition will be held, and a report will be submitted to the party and government agencies in advance, requesting that personnel be sent to provide guidance at that time. The slogans and banners for the petition parade will be prepared at the next standing committee meeting. Next, the committee discussed expanding publicity, issuing a declaration, and decided on the name "Rongguang Newspaper Gao An Special Issue". The publication date was passed as the 5th of each month. Next, the committee discussed expanding unity and decided that as long as the Gao case is not resolved satisfactorily, we, the industry, will not stop taking action until the final victory is achieved to protect the right to survival of our nation. Next, the committee discussed the legal proceedings and requested the Yangzhou Association and other associations, the Gao case support group, and various major lawyers to seek legal remedies. However, regarding mediation, Chairman Du of the French Concession Taxpayers' Association was requested to proceed as soon as possible to achieve a peaceful resolution. Next, Gao Yuanlin, the father of the deceased, reported the difficult living conditions. Next, Guo Wanhai reported the industry's donation situation. After the above cases were discussed and decided, the chairman reported on the income and expenditure accounts. The discussion continued until about 1:00 PM, when the meeting was adjourned.

Municipal Ferry Launches Night Cruises for Cool Relief 130

A New Path for Shanghai Residents to Enjoy the Cool

The municipal ferry on the Huangpu River recently launched a night cruise service for cool relief, as the summer season has arrived and the heat is gradually increasing, in order to facilitate the people of Shanghai to escape the heat in the evening. At 8:30 PM, the ferry departs from the bronze statue pier on the Bund of Nanjing Road and arrives at Gaoqiao at 10:00 PM. At 11:15 PM, it departs from Gaoqiao and returns to Shanghai at 12:30 AM. The fare is 50 cents one way for first class, and 80 cents round trip. The fare is 1 dollar one way for special class, and 1.6 dollars round trip. Regardless of the weather, rain or shine, or the number of passengers, the ferry will depart on time. The ship is decorated with colorful lights and potted flowers, and there is also wireless radio music to entertain passengers. Drinks and food of all kinds are available for passengers to purchase. From now on, people in this city can avoid the suffering of the humid heat at night and enjoy the pleasure of a clear cruise on the river, which will undoubtedly benefit their physical and mental well-being.

Mental Hospital to Open Soon 131

Dr. Gu Wenjun, an expert in treating mental illness in this area, is a seventh-generation doctor in Chuansha, specializing in the treatment of dementia, scrofula, shortness of breath, phlegm, asthma, and other diseases. He has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for nearly 30 years and has long been renowned. Dr. Gu recently observed that although there are many hospitals in Shanghai, there is still a lack of specialized treatment places for mental illnesses. In recent years, national disasters have been frequent, and many people are unemployed. It is often heard that they are in financial straits and suffer from external stimuli, causing them to become mentally ill due to anxiety. If not treated immediately, they will become disabled in mild cases and lose their lives in severe cases. Dr. Gu has a benevolent heart and deeply sympathizes with them. Therefore, he gathered colleagues Yuan Xiluo, Xie Qianggong, Wu Zonglian, Qiao Nianchun, Pan Yu Cang, and Pan Shiqing to initiate the organization of a specialized mental hospital. After several months of preparation, things have gradually come to fruition. Houses No. 22, 23, and 24 in Ren'an Lane, Guling Road, have been leased as the hospital site. All the start-up expenses are initially advanced by the initiators, and the amount is quite considerable. It is reported that philanthropists such as Xu Shiying, Wang Yiting, Du Yuesheng, Huang Jinrong, Zhang Xiaolin, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, and other gentlemen, as well as Duan Feihe, Li Sihao, and other celebrities, all support Dr. Gu's initiative, which is purely for the benefit of the poor and sick. The hospital is said to officially open at the end of this month.

Tragedy as Man Dies After Jumping Off Moving Vehicle to Retrieve Hat 140

Wang Yujiang, a 52-year-old native of Ningbo, lived at No. 68 Beikaier Road and earned his living by selling vegetables. The other day, he and more than a dozen companions were traveling to the Xiaodongmen vegetable market in Nanshi on a truck numbered 16536 to sell vegetables. On the way back, when the truck was driving near Liaoyang Road on Huade Road, Wang's hat was suddenly blown off by the wind. Wang, in a moment of panic, disregarded everything and jumped off the truck in an attempt to retrieve the hat, causing him to be crushed by the truck's wheels on his feet and other places, suffering severe injuries. His companions immediately took him to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment, but he died soon after. The hospital reported the incident to the Yulin Road Police Station, who ordered detectives to investigate. The body was taken to the Feilun Road morgue for examination. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, arrived at the morgue, examined the body, and conducted a public hearing. According to Huang Jinqing, a vegetable seller, he was sitting in the same car with Wang on that day, and Wang did not tell the others when he jumped off to pick up his hat, so the driver was also unaware, which led to this unfortunate incident. Wu Yuming, the truck driver, stated that the deceased did not order him to stop at the time, so he was not aware of the situation. After obtaining the statements, Guo ruled that the deceased, Wang Yujiang, had died due to injuries to his feet caused by being crushed before his death. The body was handed over to his wife, Wang Sangshi, who signed a guarantee to take the body back for burial.

Part of the Russian Detachment of the Businessmen's Corps Relocates to the Target Range 141

Decision on Building Permanent Barracks Temporarily Postponed

The commander of the Public Concession Businessmen's Corps reported to the Security Committee that the Public Bureau houses at the Xiamen Road prison site would soon be demolished, and that one detachment of the Russian personnel currently stationed in the wooden houses there had been temporarily transferred to the barracks at the target range. By the beginning of September, when the wooden houses at the target range were needed for other purposes, the wooden houses on Xiamen Road could be moved to the target range as well. The cost of this relocation was estimated at 7,000 taels. When new buildings were rebuilt on the Xiamen Road base, a permanent residence should be provided for the entire Russian detachment. The head of the finance department said that he agreed with the relocation of the wooden houses, but the issue of permanent barracks could be discussed when the construction plan for 1934 was proposed. The head of the public works department then presented drawings for the reconstruction of the Xiamen Road site, in which the intermediate section was planned to be used for permanent barracks, but it would not be possible to start until 1935. The permanent relocation of the wooden houses to the target range was also feasible, and the maintenance costs would not be high, and the relocation would only take a few weeks. After deliberation, the committee believed that a portion of the Xiamen Road base should be used for barracks in the future, and that the existing wooden houses should be moved to the target range immediately. When the Russian detachment no longer needed them, they would remain there for the public use of the Businessmen's Corps. This case was submitted to the board of directors and has been adopted and implemented.

Fortune-telling Stall Is a Gambling Den 142

Qi Genlin's Wild Idea

Police Find Real Evidence

Recently, fortune telling stalls, gambling dens, and ships for gambling on the Huangpu River have sprung up in the Nanshi area. However, due to the strict investigation and prohibition by the authorities, in order to avoid attention, the gangs send their members out daily to lure people into gambling, disguising themselves as workers and other types of people. Qi Genlin, a native of Nanjing, is 25 years old and lives at No. 14 Zhaoma Road, 16th Shop, Nanshi. Qi is inherently part of this trade. He recently had a wild idea to disguise himself as a fortune teller and set up a fortune-telling stall on the sidewalk in front of Hengda Ginseng Shop at No. 64 Zhonghua Road, Xiaodongmen, claiming to help people interpret characters, tell fortunes, and read faces, but in reality, the almanacs and books on physiognomy placed on his stall all contained gambling receipts for gambling and detailed dream books. He secretly lured ignorant men and women to interpret their dreams and gamble on gambling. The gambling money he collected was sent to the big factory. Qi personally made a profit of more than ten yuan every day, leading a comfortable life without anyone noticing, and he felt complacent. Unexpectedly, his good luck did not last long. Director Liu of the First District, Second Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau learned of the situation and dispatched police officer Gong Weichuan, Li Fuyi, and others to the site at about 11:00 AM yesterday to arrest Qi Genlin. They confiscated a large number of gambling receipts and gambling money from his stall and took them back to the station along with the fortune-telling stall. After the director's preliminary interrogation, the case will be reviewed and handled.

A Lewd Woman Openly Stealing a Man 143

The Husband Could No Longer Endure It

Resulting in a Severe Beating

Huang Achang, a 32-year-old paint worker from Wenzhou, residing at No. 747, Xin Kang Li, Yangshupu Road, is currently unemployed at home. His wife, Lin Afeng, 23 years old, is particularly romantic, lewd, and unrestrained. She became acquainted with a man named Xu Arong, 28 years old, who works as a tea server at lawyer Yin Ruxiong's office on Beijing Road, and earns quite well. Initially, Lin and Xu's affair was conducted discreetly, to preserve Huang Achang's reputation. However, since Huang became unemployed, Afeng became completely uninhibited, frequently inviting Xu to her home for secret rendezvous, causing gossip and spreading scandalous rumors. The night before last (the 5th), Xu went to Afeng's house again to continue their pleasure, and did not leave until midnight, causing Huang to become unbearably angry and enraged. He grabbed Xu, and with fists and feet, beat him, injuring his chest, limbs, back, and other areas, leaving him covered in wounds. Afterward, Xu went outside to report the incident to the police, and was taken along with Huang to the Yulin Road police station for investigation. The injured woman was transferred to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Robbers Sentenced Separately 144

Zhang Zhiqiong, the Chinese detective chief of the Hongkou Police Station, and detective Yin Zhanqing, previously apprehended four robbers from Suzhou—Shi Xingbao, Lu Cailin, Wang Wenqing, and Wang Ada—at No. 158 Connaught Road and No. 257 Avenue de Miniac in the French Concession, etc., confiscating a handgun and six bullets. The suspects, Zhang Afu, a woman named Lu Baoshi, and Wang Lushi, were also taken to the police station. The investigation revealed that Shi and his gang had committed armed robberies in the spring of this year, targeting Wang Li's residence at No. 146 Hongkou Road and the residence of Li Xushi, a woman at No. 349 Baike Road, stealing property worth several hundred yuan. The case was handed over to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District, where Judge Xiao Xiebin presided over the trial. After several interrogations, a verdict was scheduled for pronouncement. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao of the Special Court presided over the pronouncement of the judgment. Defendants Shi Xingbao, Lu Cailin, Wang Wenqing, and Wang Ada were each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention were allowed to be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The handgun and bullets were confiscated. Zhang Afu, Lu Baoshi, and Wang Lushi were all found not guilty. The police station's lawyer declared that they would waive the right to appeal the acquittal, and they were immediately released.

Rapist and Conspirator Sentenced 145

Wang Agen to Seven Years, Chen Zhushi to Five Years

Chen Zhushi, a woman who abducts women, lured a 16-year-old girl named Ashun from Carter Road to the Southeast Hotel. There, Wang Agen, also known as Wang Ada, and an accomplice, raped her first. The next day, Chen Zhushi took her to the Shun Tian Steamboat exit for sale, where she was discovered and rescued by Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang, investigators from the Relief Society.

The District Court dispatched police to arrest Wang Agen. Prosecutor Xie investigated and brought charges. Judge Yang examined the case thoroughly, stating that the defendants had conspired to profit by luring a person into a living hell, and that the victim was raped and her chastity violated, their crimes were heinous. Moreover, Ashun was not yet sixteen years old. Therefore, yesterday's verdict sentenced Wang Agen to seven years of imprisonment and Chen Zhushi to five years of imprisonment. The defendants disagreed with the verdict and were remanded into custody.

Young Man Attempts Suicide in the River, Rescued 146

Yesterday at around 9 a.m., a young man boarded the No. 10 ferry at the New Customs Wharf on Hankou Road, seemingly intending to cross to Pudong. Unexpectedly, as the boat reached mid-stream, the man suddenly jumped into the river, intending to commit suicide. Fortunately, Chinese police officers 98 and 118 from the Customs Water Police Station were patrolling in a motorboat and managed to rescue him. They took him to the police station, where he identified himself as Wang Fengqi, 19 years old, from Shandong. He had recently come to Shanghai from Jiangbei to seek work with a friend, but he did not know his friend's address. For several days, he had been running out of money and had no one to turn to for help, so he decided to end his life. The police chief, finding him very pitiable, assigned detective Xu Juenian to send him to the Shandong Fellow Villagers Association for assistance.

City News 152

China Industrial Bank's Improved Prize Savings. The China Industrial Bank has been operating prize savings since it was approved by the Ministry of Finance in 1919. It has enjoyed a good reputation and the trust of society. Now, in order to seek progress and benefit the people's livelihood, the bank has further improved its regulations. The method is that the payment only needs to be made once, to save the trouble of monthly payments. The deposit amount can be as high as 30 yuan per household or as low as 3 yuan. All prizes are provided by the bank and do not take a share of the savings. This is a unique feature that sets the bank apart from others. The principal is repaid in eight years, with interest. Each deposit entitles the depositor to 32 chances of winning a 10,000-yuan prize over eight years. In addition, funds can be pledged after one year and can be returned with additional interest after four years. The favorable treatment of depositors truly opens a new era in the savings industry.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the coastal areas of Shandong, the Yangtze River Basin, and areas south of Ma'anshan would be mostly cloudy with gentle or brisk northeasterly to southeasterly winds. Anhui Huaining District Examination Dispute Resolved 160

The dispute over the Anhui Huaining District Secondary School Examination has been reported in previous reports. On July 1, when the examination began, students said that the test questions had been leaked and filed a lawsuit in court. At that time, all male high school and junior high school students completely boycotted the exam, while only female students took the exam as usual. However, students from Anqing Middle School and other schools who took the exam were unwilling to boycott the exam and were beaten by students from other schools who were exempted from the exam, so they went to the Education Department to take refuge and took the exam in the Education Department on the 2nd. High school students from other counties negotiated with the Education Department to return to their schools to take the exam separately under the supervision of the Education Department. The students from the four schools of Anqing No. 1 Middle School, Huaining Middle School, Liuyi Middle School, and Baoluo Middle School boycotted the exam from beginning to end. The provincial government decided not to allow students from these schools to take the exam again and severely punish the students who took the lead in causing trouble. The high school students also boycotted the exam most strongly at the beginning. Yesterday, they confessed their mistakes to the Education Department, and the Education Department has allowed them to take a makeup exam. Also, Guo Xianzhong, the principal of Anqing Middle School, was slightly injured by the boycotting students for leading the students to take the exam. In this case, the dispute over the Huaining District Examination can be completely resolved.

National Vocational Education Association Discusses the Issue of Implementing Vocational Education in Prisons 162

The National Vocational Education Discussion Conference is scheduled to be held in Kaifeng on the 9th of this month. The details have been reported in this newspaper. The conference will have a precise discussion on the issue of implementing vocational education in prisons in various regions. Once a decision is made, it will be submitted to the Judicial and Administrative Department for circulation and implementation. The full text of the case is recorded below for reference.

According to the general evaluation of sociologists, the causes of crime can be generally said to be nothing more than sexual desire and economic problems, but among the two problems, economic problems are the root cause. Modern prisons are not only institutions for enforcing punishment, but also places for rehabilitation. Therefore, most prisons in modern cities have factories attached to them, so that prisoners can learn relevant vocational education skills, so that they can have a means of making a living after being released from prison. This is really a fundamental way to clear crimes, but according to on-the-spot investigations, the vocational education in prisons in our country now mostly does not conform to the principles of education, has no scientific methods, and the prisons with factories are limited to large cities. There are very few county towns with prison factories. The association should try to improve the factories in prisons in large cities and implement vocational education in county prisons without factories. The method is that the research department of the association should study the specific plan for the implementation of vocational education in prisons and submit it to the Judicial and Administrative Department for circulation to prisons in various cities and counties to earnestly implement vocational education.

Shanghai Municipal Education Museum Soliciting Songs 164

The Deadline is the 23rd of this Month

All Selected Manuscripts Will Be Rewarded

The Shanghai Municipal Education Museum is initiating the solicitation of improved songs in order to improve folk songs and promote public art. The methods are as follows: 1. In order to improve folk songs and promote public art, the museum is soliciting entries from all people who meet the following criteria. 2. All folk songs that contain the following meanings, whether original or old works, are welcome: A. Health and sports, B. Literacy, C. Thrift, D. National defense, E. Improvement of customs. 3. All lyrics and melodies should be simple and easy to sing. 4. Contributors must submit at least two types of songs. 5. The deadline is July 23. 6. Contributors must write the sheet music and lyrics clearly. 7. Manuscripts should be sent to the museum at the Confucian Temple Road in Ximen. 8. The museum will invite people to evaluate and announce the results in the newspaper. 9. The museum will provide a small remuneration for all selected manuscripts.

The address is located in the high school department of the Shanghai Girls' High School on Lin Yin Road, Ximen. The houses are spacious and can provide accommodation. There are still vacancies. Those who are interested in learning should register as soon as possible.

Wuben Faculty and Staff Say Farewell to Cao Yihua 172

Since Mr. Cao Yihua took office as the director of studies at Wuben Girls' High School, he has made many reforms in the past three years and has won the trust of the principal. Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Government announced that he would be the principal of Donghai Normal School. The Wuben faculty and staff could not retain him and deeply regretted his departure. Therefore, at 6 pm yesterday, they held a banquet at Yizhixiang to bid him farewell. During the banquet, Lu An and Wang Peizhen delivered speeches successively, which were followed by a thank you speech by Mr. Cao. He said that Donghai is located in the northeast of Jiangsu Province, close to Shandong. The customs and habits of the people are very strong towards the north, which is different from the situation where the north-south culture has been opened up. Moreover, this school has been divided into 18 grades. Since it was changed to a normal school, there are only 12 grades in the high and junior two departments with six classes each. Although the students who come to study are poor, the study style is noisy and very difficult to manage, which is completely different from Wuben. For the sake of cultivating teachers, I will make every effort to rectify it, so as to create normal school talents for the country and society, so as to achieve the effect of popularizing education in the future. As for the employment of teachers, I advocate talentism, and so on. The banquet ended at about 10 o'clock.

Business Leaders Retain President Xu of the Business School 173

Since Mr. Xu Peikun became the president of the National Shanghai Business School, he has achieved remarkable results, and talents have emerged in large numbers over the years, making great contributions to the society. Recently, someone incited a wave of unrest, hoping to disrupt Mr. Xu's work. He was so overwhelmed that he suddenly had the intention of retiring. Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Qian Xinzhi and other business leaders in Shanghai believed that the Business School was the highest business school in Shanghai. Mr. Xu had been the president for many years and had made many plans. Once he retired, all his previous efforts would be wasted. Recently, someone has incited a wave of unrest, hoping to disrupt it. Please telegraph Education Minister Wang to protect it, so that Shanghai's highest business school can continue to develop as usual. I am very grateful and hope so. In addition to telegraphing Education Minister Wang, I hereby telegraph this and pray for a reply. Yu Hede, Wang Xiaolai, Qian Yongming, and others kowtow." It is reported that Chairman Jiang has replied to Shanghai, saying that the Ministry of Education will be able to handle it fairly. Yu and others are very satisfied. On the one hand, they have been trying to persuade Mr. Xu not to retire. According to the New Voice Agency, the Shanghai Business School has always been very short of funds, and all facilities have not been able to proceed actively on schedule. President Xu Peikun felt the difficulty of having no rice to cook and once expressed his negativity to the former Education Minister Zhu. Last week, he went to Beijing to meet Education Minister Wang Shijie and reiterated his previous request. After Education Minister Wang earnestly retained him and persuaded him from various parties, Mr. Xu returned to the school to preside over the school affairs, considering that he had been in the education sector for nearly 20 years and that the overall education plan was a matter of responsibility, especially during the national crisis. He should make efforts to maintain it, and he returned to the school that day to preside over the school affairs and carry out all the school affairs for the next semester.

News from the China Correspondence School of Accountancy 174

The China Correspondence School of Accountancy, located at 1154 Xinzha Road, Shanghai, was founded by Accountant Shen Liren and has been painstakingly managed with remarkable results. The compilation of the school's textbooks for each subject is the most novel. It is said that the compilation was preceded by a long period of research and trial-and-error methods. The compiled textbooks were given to those who did not know bookkeeping and accounting to read and test them, and only after they were thoroughly understood. Therefore, the compilation of the textbooks is very different from the ordinary readers on the market. They are specially compiled for correspondence courses. Since the school was opened, the total number of students has reached more than 2,000, and the first edition of the textbooks has been sold out. For the sake of excellence, Accountant Shen took the opportunity of the reprinting to revise the contents of each subject and made many improvements. It is reported that the reprinted textbooks have been printed a few days ago. In order to collect opinions and use them for reference, Accountant Shen specially gave many copies of the new edition of the textbooks to domestic accounting groups, educational institutions and accounting experts to solicit criticism. Recently, he has received replies from all parties, praising its proper compilation, clear and willing language, detailed examples, and exquisite printing, making it the only good book for accounting correspondence in China. The school also has trial reading materials for those who are interested in studying bookkeeping and accounting.

Wimbledon Men's Singles Vines and Crawford to Compete for the Championship 177

Vines Defeats Cochet 3-1

Crawford Defeats Sato 3-1

(London, 5th, Reuters) Vines, the US Champion and Wimbledon Champion, displayed his genius for leadership in the Wimbledon Men's Singles Semi-Final today with a fierce and formidable attack, eliminating the French Championship Player Henri Cochet, the score being 6-2, 8-6, 3-6, 6-1. Meanwhile, Crawford beat Japan's Sato in another group and also won the right to the final, the score being 6-3, 6-4, 2-6, 6-4.

Vines vs. Cochet 178

After giving up the first set, Cochet showed obvious improvement in the second set, serving more powerfully and returning the opponent's serves more effectively. The left and right cross-shots almost made Vines's pace chaotic, and he once led 5-2. But at this point, Vines began to use cannonballs and explosive pressure to make Cochet confused. In the second set, Vines won again 8-6. Cochet won back the third set 6-3, and Vines succeeded greatly with 6-1.

Crawford vs. Sato 179

Crawford eliminated the Japanese Sato 6-3, 6-4, 2-6, 6-4, and will compete with Vines for the championship. Crawford's long shots are extremely deep, often causing the white belt on the baseline to bounce up. Sato ran around, hoping to save it, but in the end he collapsed and was defeated by Crawford.

The North China Games Are About to Open 186

To be held in Qingdao from the 12th to the 15th of this month

The architectural form of the venue is magnificent and can be called unparalleled in China

(Qingdao Correspondence) The North China Sports Federation, which bears a major mission in the Chinese sports world, has been working hard to hold sports games for many years, and has held 17 sessions so far. Its long history has promoted the development of the national spirit in China, which is not shallow. Since the 17th session was decided to be held in Qingdao this year, Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie said that the holding of the conference is related to the development of sports in the city. In addition to telegraphing the North China Sports Federation to express his welcome, he immediately began to build a large-scale public sports field for the conference. On the one hand, he hired people from all walks of life to organize a preparatory committee. Now, the opening of the conference is less than ten days away (July 12-15). The construction of the venue and the preparation of the conference affairs are described as follows:

Overview of the Venue Qingdao has the beauty of mountains and seas, and the construction of the North China venue is located in the center of the beautiful scenery. The venue includes a track and field field (including a football field), six tennis courts, four volleyball courts (also used as a martial arts field), a baseball field, and a swimming pool using the natural seaside and adding appropriate facilities. The main track and field field is modeled after the Los Angeles World Sports Field in the United States, which is concrete and subtle, but the magnificence of the project and the beauty of the environment are unparalleled by sports fields in other parts of the country. The situation is described as follows: ㈠ The form of the stands is determined by the form of the track. The length of the outer circle is more than 590 meters, and the length of the inner circle is more than 540 meters. The entire venue is symmetrically arranged east and west. There are a total of 15 rows of seats for the audience, which can accommodate more than 15,000 spectators. The audience seats are made of reinforced concrete. The inner and outer walls of the stands are made of granite ice crack lines. There are 11 entrance doors for spectators and 2 entrance doors for athletes around the stands except for the main entrance. There are 4 entrances and exits for athletes in the inner circle of the stands. All of the stands under the east, west and south straight lines are used for athletes to rest. There are 32 rest rooms, 4 bathrooms, and 8 male and female toilets. Each entrance door for spectators has 1 male and female toilet. There are a total of 30 toilets. The middle part of the east and west sides of the stands is the rostrum and the VIP seats. ㈡ The form of the track is blue curved, also known as the normal form, which was created by German Dr. Timm. The straight part is 130 meters long and the field is 72 meters wide. If measured along the outer three centimeters of the inner circle of the track, the length of one circle is exactly 400 meters. The suitability of the form goes without saying. Each field event is arranged in it. The entire field is covered with grass except for the track and field events, which is especially beautiful. ㈢ The main entrance of the track and field field is located at the north end of the stands, with a total of three floors. The first floor is the aisle, and there are three arched entrance doors. The second floor is the conference hall, and the third floor is the office. There is a large clock in the center of the roof, which is very convenient. It takes 11 steps to climb from the west road to the first floor of the main entrance, which is about 2 meters high, so pedestrians on the road cannot see the movements of the athletes in the field.

Preparation Situation The Preparatory Committee of the 17th North China Games was organized by the city government by hiring people from all walks of life in the city. Lei Fazhang (Director of the Education Bureau) was elected as the director of the preparation, and Hao Gengsheng (Director of Physical Education of Shandong University) was the general secretary. The preparatory committee is divided into ten departments: General Affairs, Competition, Engineering Reception, Arrangement, Publicity, Awards, Health, Discipline, and Martial Arts. Each department has a director and deputy director, who are responsible for the progress respectively. Since the establishment of the preparatory committee, four preparatory meetings have been held. The joint meetings of each department were initially held once every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday. Later, due to the approaching date of the conference, it was changed to working at the preparatory committee every day. The budget of the conference, excluding the engineering item, is a total of more than 39,100 yuan. With regard to the reception, Mayor Shen Honglie, in order to give the participants of each unit a good impression, everything must be done carefully. The athlete reception method, the referee reception method, and the press reporter reception method have all been carefully planned and stipulated. Therefore, the North China Conference held in the beautiful Qingdao enjoys comfortable reception. At that time, the athletes from the provinces and cities of North China will gallop on the field, which is a great event for the future development of the North China Conference.

Joint Meeting The venue project is about to be completed, and the opening of the conference is imminent. In order to understand the situation of the venue and step up their work, the preparatory committee inspected the venue project at 11 am on the 3rd and took a group photo. After lunch at the male athlete dormitory, the fourth preparatory meeting was held. The directors of each department attended the meeting. Mayor Shen Honglie also participated. After the meeting, the directors of each department reported on the status of the work of each department. Then Mayor Shen gave instructions on the matters that each department should pay attention to. Then they began to discuss the matters that should be carried out at the conference, and the meeting did not end until 5 pm. All the preparatory staff were in high spirits. The conference can be said to have gained the advantages of people and harmony.

Participating in the Grand Event Because the conference is held in Qingdao, the provinces, cities, and regions of North China are actively participating. After the registration deadline, the total number of participating units includes Shandong, Shanxi, Henan, Hebei, Shaanxi, Suiyuan, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Beiping, Qingdao, Weihai, and other twelve provinces, cities, and regions. There are 715 male athletes and 319 female athletes, totaling 1,034. It is expected that the conference will be more enthusiastic than the 16th session. What is worth commemorating is that although the recovery of the Northeast has no date, the athletes of the three northeastern provinces are still working hard to participate, hoping to make the flags of the provinces fly at the conference site, so as to encourage the Chinese people. Therefore, the significance of holding this conference is not only to promote physical education, but also for the Chinese people to rise up.
