Spring and Autumn

Fish and Geese Eat Lawsuits 189

— Zhan Lu

Should Invite Wang Shifu to be the Defense Lawyer

Among the myriad of strange occurrences on the Shanghai Bund, there is a bizarre story of a postman colluding with two young men to privately open letters sent to a young woman.

Postman Ye Woyun of number 166 is too meddlesome; how could he not deliver letters sent to a young woman to the young woman, but instead give them to irrelevant wicked youths to peek at next to the leather tanning stall in the alleyway? Now that the matter has been confirmed, he has been detained and sent to the criminal court, prosecuted for the crime of obstructing privacy under Article 333 of the Criminal Law. This is Ye Woyun bringing disaster upon himself, and everyone believes he should be severely punished.

Love letters on postcards can certainly be enjoyed first by the green-clad messenger; the sender has paid a little more postage, and once sealed with paste, has obtained the right to secret freedom. The postman has the obligation to deliver letters, but no right to open them. The criminal charges Ye Woyun has committed are very difficult to defend him against. If one wants to defend him, one would have to summon Hongniang from the "Romance of the Western Chamber".

In the "Noisy Chapters", Hongniang sings, "When have you ever seen someone sending letters secretly hiding them from the fish and geese?" Since Hongniang says so, it can be seen that the sender in Hongniang's mind should not hide the contents of the letter from the fish and geese; and those who act as fish and geese have the right to know the secrets in the sender's letter. Ye Woyun acts as a postman, which is acting as a fish and goose. If he can invite Sister Hongniang, who transmits letters and delivers messages, to be his defense attorney, and present "When have you ever seen someone sending letters secretly hiding them from the fish and geese?" as the major reason for the defense, I think Ye Woyun can certainly be declared innocent. Moreover, Sister Hongniang has profound legal knowledge. "Meixiang punishes the quince" was all Sister Hongniang declaring the sentence for the young lady when "cleverly sitting in court." With such eloquence, to reverse the injustice for Ye Woyun, there would naturally be no such thing as fish and geese eating lawsuits.

However, the author of "Romance of the Western Chamber" is generally known to be Mr. Wang Shifu. Rather than inviting Sister Hongniang to be the defense attorney, it would be better to invite Mr. Wang Shifu to be the defense attorney; only because the words in Hongniang's mouth are the articles under Wang Shifu's pen. Jin Shengtan, in his criticism of "Romance of the Western Chamber," most admired this sentence, "When have you ever seen someone sending letters secretly hiding them from the fish and geese?" He commented, "Strange, strange, wonderful, wonderful, from Pangu until this day, there has truly never been such a thing, nor has there ever been such writing." Wang Shifu's magical power of words can make Shengtan this kind of disoriented, which is certainly not easy to do.

Ye Woyun, who is eating a lawsuit, doesn't need to be afraid. Quickly go to the world of six hundred years ago and invite this Yuan Dynasty lyricist, Mr. Wang Shifu, to be your pro bono lawyer, and you can escape unscathed.

Lullaby 190

— Ye Yi-yi

"Don't be noisy, don't make a fuss, baby wants to sleep."

This is a section of a very popular lullaby in Shanghai. Almost everyone has heard it; every young student and every woman knows how to sing it!

If you run to the dazzling crossroads, then you can hear the various ballads and songs broadcast on the radio in front of the big stores. Many people will gather together spontaneously, raising their heads to listen. But the strange thing is, you raise your head to listen, and sometimes, a nasal lullaby will play in that little wooden box; whether it is in the morning or afternoon, it will always lull you to sleep with "Don't be noisy, don't make a fuss, baby wants to sleep"! In reality, you can't sleep, right?

Some merchants still hire military bands to blow big drums there; however, they are also very fashionable, blowing and beating lullabies; if you run from far away, you can hear the sounds of "dee dee dee" and "dong dong dong"!

Ah! Our compatriots originally all like to be fashionable! But in general, they will blindly copy patterns; and not know whether this matter is appropriate or not?

Japanese soldiers have invaded a section of our country's territory, so telegrams and shouts, meetings and cries, seem to be very patriotic; but what is the use of this kind of irrelevant thing? Perhaps it is because of this reason, so there is the rise of the lullaby by clever people, intending to avoid the turbulent world, but I hope this lullaby does not wake people up.

Let the compatriots sleep forever, sleep for a thousand days and a thousand years; it's good to wait until they wake up in the future, the Japanese will bring face wash water to wash your face and prepare breakfast for you to eat.

Philosophy of Love 191

— Yi Qiu

When you first attack her, she is indeed an exceptionally noble and mysterious woman; but, after your hope is realized, all her nobility and mystery will naturally disappear!

If you suffer the arrogance of a proud woman, you must patiently strive to pursue her. Once you are victorious, the day she loves you is the time for your revenge!

The clock is the most cunning thing. When you have a date with your lover, it will definitely hesitate to move forward, deliberately making things difficult for you; but after you meet your lover, it will run wildly in quick steps. Ah! Clock! You really know how to play with people!

When you hold your lover's slender waist and walk slowly on the street, all the scenery is set up for you; but after you are lovelorn, that beautiful scenery will suddenly turn into a desolate ruin!

Summer Streets 192

— Huang Kewei

The summer sun has set a fire, and the asphalt roads are all scorched! The rickshaw pullers are barefoot, running like ants on a hot pot!

"Damn it! Murderous bastard! Running so slow!" The curse of a woman with bare thighs.

"Pull faster! Pig!" The curse of an urban young master.

Soybean-sized beads of sweat drip straight down, the soles of the feet stepping on the hot road are blistering, but for the price of two dimes, to support their wives, children, and daughters, they have to risk their lives to pull!

The ice banner, crying with a sad face in the sunlight, large glass windows display ice cream, soda, shaved ice, roses, bananas, lemons...

Red lips, holding white straws, dim green lights, reflecting simply dressed waiters, electric fans turning, ice machines flowing, standing on the street, entering an ice room is at least thirty degrees cooler.

Clear and cool mung bean soup, jelly, cold noodles, watermelon stalls, green bottle flies buzzing around, flying back and forth. On the electric poles, there are posters: "Prevent Cholera"! Standing under the traffic lights, the red-headed Indian, sweating, his multi-bearded purple face, has also been tanned by the red sun!

A modern girl holds up a pink parasol, covering the upper half of her body, in a thin silk cheongsam, still shaking her head and shouting that it's hot.

A pug sticks out its long tongue and pants, saliva flows to the ground, and it dries with a "zhi" sound.

In the corner, a small beggar, naked, has come to a public model.

Come On! Have a Cup of Ice Cream 193

— Rong Yu

Come on, have a cup of ice cream, in the hot weather,

When you are dripping with sweat, everyone loves to hear these words.

But ice cream also has different grades. In noble cold drink shops, drinking a cup might cost a good few dimes, plus a tip, which isn't a poor person's daily ration? The ten-cent-a-cup shouted along the street is probably unreliable. If you drink it, you will definitely sit in a white car and be sent to the epidemic hospital. Even more severely, it may freeze your forehead, freezing down to your heels. It's really not worth it to be greedy and lose your poor life!

Forget it! With your kind of publicity, cold drink shop owners are afraid to fight with you to the death; people who love cold drinks may not take these words as golden rules. Now I also have a cup of ice cream to offer to everyone.

In the "Notes from the Thatched Cottage of Close Observations" written by Mr. Ji Xiaolan,

There is a passage that says: "A certain scholar's study was narrow and cramped, almost impossible to raise his head. The door had no curtain, the bed had no mosquito net, the courtyard had no trees. After a long drought, it was hot and humid, as if sitting in a steaming pot. He took off his clothes for an afternoon nap, but the flies were disturbing him and he couldn't close his eyes. He was so annoyed that he could hardly bear it, and he thought of this as a fiery hell. After a long time, he fell asleep from exhaustion. He dreamed of riding a boat in the sea. A hurricane suddenly arose, the sky and sun were dark, the masts were broken and the sails were torn, and he was terrified. In an instant, the boat capsized. It seemed someone pulled him out and threw him on the shore. Then someone held a rope to bind him and locked him in a cellar. It was dark and he couldn't see anything, and his breathing was also suffocated and blocked. The horror and distress were indescribable. Suddenly, he heard a shout in his ear. He suddenly opened his eyes, and he was still lying on the three-legged wooden bed. He felt comfortable in his limbs and refreshed in his mind, as if he were in a fairyland."

The residents of Shanghai all live in pigeon coop-like houses, and their annoyance is almost the same as that of the scholar. When you are too hot to bear, please read the above passage, and I know that many people will put their hands together and recite:

Cool! Cool! It is sweet dew, it is ice cream, the heat is completely gone, together we ascend to a cool world.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 194

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Ten: Hearing the words, Jingfang's heart quickens, the wish to be ennobled is vague, listening to songs reveals emotion, serving the country is leisurely. Thinking like this, during the five-minute break on the stage, Guizhi finally couldn't bear it and smiled and asked Man Ying: "What is the name of this brigade commander?" Man Ying said: "His surname is Ma. Two years ago, he wasn't very rich. Luck came and he became a brigade commander within two years." Guizhi said: "Aren't the affairs of the three northeastern provinces not yet settled? Soldiers should all be busy. How can he have time to listen to operas? I see your Company Commander Tian. To enter the city once, you have to wait a week. He is still busy coming and going. How can someone who has become a brigade commander be so leisurely?" Man Ying smiled and said: "Company Commander Tian is just Company Commander Tian. Why do you bring up you two? I don't lead troops, where does the company commander come from?" Guizhi glanced at him and smiled, "I'm not wrong." Man Ying smiled, "It doesn't matter if you're wrong, it doesn't matter to me." Guizhi didn't want to chat idly, and brought the topic back to the main point, saying: "I heard that it's not easy for a company commander to be promoted to a brigade commander." Man Ying said: "That depends on a person's luck. When that person's luck comes, closing the door won't stop it. If the superior wants to promote him, what can you do?" Guizhi said: "He just got promoted out of thin air like this, hasn't he fought in any battles?" Man Ying said: "Look at his handsome young appearance, can he fight in battles?" Guizhi said: "According to you, there are also soldiers who pick up an official to do." Man Ying said: "Who says there aren't? " Jiangshi heard the young lady always asking about that brigade commander, as if she admired him very much. Her heart moved, and she said, "Originally, now only doing military work is the easiest to get promoted and become rich." Guizhi said: "If the military officers were all like this Brigade Commander Ma, bringing a new wife to listen to operas, then it would be okay to do it." These few words of hers were generally speaking about people, but when Huang Man Ying heard them, he already understood her interests. (122)

Miscellaneous Talk

Summer in Shanghai 195

— Ke Ding'an

The God of Time tells us, "I have advanced into summer." In this way, the scene of a fiery umbrella hanging high and hot air everywhere seems to unfold before our eyes. I am most afraid of the heat. The source of heat is emitted from the sunlight. To put it simply, I am afraid of "white." How fierce it is, how cruel. Good green grass, given a shine by it, changes color; good flowers, given a shine by it, immediately lower their heads. Little birds, given a shine by it, will stop singing; little yellow dogs, given a shine by it, will stick out their tongues. Even people, seeing it, will not dare to go out. The only thing that agrees with it is the stench-chasing fly, flying around in groups. Sun! It's rare for you to have such a good friend. Otherwise, I think you're too monotonous! Too miserable!

The compatriots in North China are certainly not in the minority. Suffering the sorrow of lost land, their families broken, their people dead! What else is there to say! These are all "sun"-given rewards. They are also like me, seeing the "sun" and being afraid, and having no resistance, and the situation is the same. But my fear of the "sun" can be sitting at home; or drinking a bottle of soda, eating a piece of watermelon. What about the compatriots in North China! Without their families, their relatives died tragically. Resistance is of course out of the question, but even their own lives are difficult to protect! Then, the same fear of the "sun," the situation is different.

○　○　○　○

"A ghost in the morning, a person dressed up in the evening." These two sentences are for the fashionable women of Shanghai. Of course, there are many who are naturally beautiful, but those like the above two sentences are as numerous as the sands of the Ganges! When they get up in the morning, their clothes are unkempt, their hair is disheveled—this may be my misunderstanding, now hair that shines like a mirror has become outdated, and curly and disheveled is the most popular style—their faces are sallow, their eyebrows are not drawn—some have shaved off both eyebrows—you would never dream that such a person would be so beautiful and charming in the evening!

After dressing up in the evening, the three-sectioned body lives in the georgette, the chest is towering forward, with a pair of milk peaks, the waist is as thin as a reed, and the lower back protrudes backward with high buttocks. In a long cheongsam, two thick legs are vaguely visible. Some even don't wear socks—if you have scars on your legs, it's better to wear a pair of socks—such a fleshy body can attract the opposite sex to chase after her. Looking at her face again, you can only see a white face, with a bright red mouth in the middle. This is comparable to vanilla ice cream with a red cherry on top. You don't need to appreciate the beauty or ugliness of her face, because if you look closely, it will make you shout out loud.

In the past, what was said above belonged to low-class women, but as the times progressed, ordinary middle-class women also have such a trend. If you don't believe it, you only need to stand at the crossroads every day, and you can always enjoy countless expressions of fleshy women. This doesn't cost money but allows you to feast your eyes on them; then there are those who spend money to watch Russian women's * dances. They are truly the biggest fools in the world!

○　○　○　○

Perhaps this is the expression of summer! In every park, every morning, there are couples of young people. Some are talking intimately, some are joking, some are flirting, some are holding hands... Almost all the programs that should be in the history of love can be seen.

However, people from another world can also be seen in every park. There are also those who practice Tai Chi, those who read books, those who sit idly, those who run, those who walk idly, and even Chinese maids pushing foreign children's carts, and Chinese women with children in general... In this way, the beautiful park cannot be exclusively occupied by lovers.

Securities 201

Dalian Agreement Signing Public Bonds Continue to Hit New Highs

96 and Whole 6 Issues Show Particularly Strong Gains

Yesterday, the trend in the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange remained positive. Amid this high level of optimism, the sudden announcement of the signing of the Dalian Agreement further strengthened market sentiment. The 96 and Whole 6 issues, in particular, showed stronger gains. This is because most people believed that the market price was already high and shorting was more advantageous. However, after settlement, the market price did not decrease and instead rose again, resulting in buying in. This back and forth raised the market price invisibly. This is one reason. During previous similar settlement periods, short squeezes often occurred, even deviating from the environment and leading to uncontrolled price increases, which were often unfavorable to short sellers. This is another reason. Forward premiums favored long positions, while short positions often faced premiums. Therefore, except for those with physical goods, speculators did not dare to attempt shorting easily. However, this does not apply to changes in the current situation. For the 96 issue, excluding the Japanese gold bonds, the actual amount was 48 million. The government previously exchanged these for new bonds, but those that were not exchanged accounted for more than one-third. The remaining majority was accumulated in the financial sector. These were bought at high prices during the 1925 96 crisis, and they cannot be sold at the current market price without exposing the truth. Therefore, the amount circulating in the market is estimated to be only around 10 million. When demand increases, there is a panic of insufficient chips. This is partly because the market price of various bonds is already high, and speculators avoid heavy positions and choose light ones. It is also partly because the surplus of customs revenue is gradually increasing, leading to rumors of consolidation. Unless one only sells when there are many physical goods and only buys when there is surplus capital, one will inevitably enter the whirlpool. Yesterday, market prices increased gradually in each of the two sessions in the morning, with gains of 3 to 4 jiao. The 96 issue gained 6 to 7 jiao. In the two afternoon sessions, highs and lows were mixed. Overall, the market remained firm and stable. Demand for Whole 6 was high, while supply was low. Although the 96 issue was heavily sold by the Northern Group, the buyers were also strong, and the market price remained firm and stable. Buying was mainly focused on the 4th and 16th issues, while selling was mainly from the 11th issue and the Northern Group. As a result, market prices consistently rose by 1 to 2 jiao to around half a yuan. The 96 issue rose by 4.5 to 6.5 jiao, and the Whole 6 issue rose by as much as 8 to 9 jiao. The market prices of various securities mostly hit new highs. The total transaction volume was 14,316,000 yuan, including 6,000 yuan in spot goods. Futures for the 96 issue accounted for the largest share, with a transaction volume of 3.34 million. Salt tax was 2,875,000, consolidated tax and the 20th issue were both 1,835,000, demobilization was 1,375,000, the 19th Customs Surtax was 1.1 million, and the 20th issue was 820,000. The remaining issues ranged from tens of thousands to 340,000.

Grain, Wheat, and Flour Show Slight Turnaround 210

Yesterday, the flour market showed a slight turnaround because factories slowed down their selling. Yesterday, in the integrated market, only Fuxin and small to medium-sized factories sold slightly in the afternoon, and the output was also small. Customer demand was slightly more active. This is because the Northern warlords are about to be resolved, and there is hope for future sales. Therefore, some scattered groups inquired, and the Andong group handled sales more actively. Both spot and forward sales were being received, and market sentiment stabilized. This attracted new long positions and short covering transactions, and the market immediately stabilized. Closing prices were large 75 for July and October, large 1.25 for August and September, and large 1 for November and December.

Yesterday, wheat turned around for all months because new long positions and short covering offset the selling pressure, and market sentiment stabilized. However, the market softened again slightly after a large trader sold in the afternoon. As a result, the large price was 3 fen for July, August, and October, large 1 fen for September, large 4 fen for November, and large 1 fen for December. 20,000 bags of spot wheat continued to arrive. Factories initially planned to continue their defensive stance, but later some traders took them back. Fuxin also handled more than 2,000 bags as a courtesy, with prices opening at 3.65 yuan to 3.4 yuan.

Small Polished Rice Sales Are Active, Up One Jiao 211

Min and Zhejiang Sales are Very Active...All Types of Rice Are Doing Well

Yesterday, the Min group sold 1,183 bags of Hunan rice, 821 bags of Nanjing and Wuxi rice, and 1,300 bags of small polished rice. The Wentai group sold 206 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice and 1,800 bags of small polished rice. Local street vendors sold 400 bags of Saigon rice and 200 bags of small polished rice. Local customers continued to be active, and market sentiment and market conditions both showed upward momentum. Small polished rice and Hunan Jinjing rice each rose by one jiao. High-quality Xiang Jing rice is already scarce, and medium-quality rice is also scarce. After the Min group searched for it, the market price immediately rose. Small polished rice has been active for several days, and 3,200 bags were offered yesterday, which is an especially good situation. Therefore, all prices rose by one jiao, and the rest showed a turnaround and followed suit.

Lower River Rice is in a Stable Situation 212

(South Shanghai) The source is more than thirty numbers, and the market situation is stable. Although sellers unanimously called for price increases, customers were unwilling to buy much due to the hot weather, resulting in a sluggish inventory in urban and rural stores. The market prices of thick japonica rice from the Chang group, Su Tong group, and Nangang, etc., showed no changes. Only Du Yangjian still showed its beauty because it was in short supply and fragrant. The Qingdao and Tianjin groups purchased only 600 to 700 bags of Qingsong Sibo rice, and the market situation was also flat. Looking at the trend near noon, it already showed signs of softening, so it is expected that there will be a price cut in tomorrow's market. Bian Yuan's stable situation changed because the Fuzhou group purchased 200 bags, and the other stomach was also good, and the market price rose by one jiao.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were about twenty sources of rice from the Lower River area. The sales of white japonica rice were normal, and the market shape was stable. Early thin rice was in short supply and sold actively, and the price saw a tightening. Sheep tip was slightly soft, Du Bu customer tip was normal, and the source of Bian Yuan was less sold and sluggish, and the market shape was fixed.

Soybean Cake Factory Market Loosens 213

Yesterday, the soybean cake factory market was still loose, but there were still 20,000 to 30,000 sales, so the market continued to defend the original market. The factory's recent price cuts were actually due to the abundance of spot goods and the unfavorable conditions of the exchange's fatigue and speculation, resulting in price cuts to seek sales. Although the market has stabilized, market sentiment has already weakened.

Free Talk

The Liberation of the Preface 219

— Tao Zhui

In feudal times, when a person wrote a book, it was "hidden in famous mountains and passed down to the right person." That's all in the past. Now it's been thirty-three years into the twentieth century, and the place is the Shanghai concession. Becoming a comprador brings immediate glory and wealth, so why shouldn't a writer immediately seek fame and fortune? Thus, there is a method.

That method is to first decide that you are a writer and have some inheritance or subsidy. Then, open your own bookstore, run your own magazine, publish your own articles, create your own advertisements, report your own news, and think up your own tricks... But it doesn't work. The liberation of poetry has already been done by someone else, and the liberation of lyrics can only fool birds. Therefore, the "liberation of the preface" arises.

The preface has existed since ancient times, written by others or by the author. But this is too old-fashioned and doesn't suit the taste of the "writer" of the "new era." Because it's difficult to boast in your own preface, and others might not necessarily flatter you, it's only natural to liberate it, which means having yourself write a preface for your own work, calling it "extracting letters," which sounds like adding flowers to brocade. A "collection of good reviews" still needs to be attached at the end, but a substitute preface allows you to see a lot of praise as soon as you open the book, like a famous actor stepping onto the stage and everyone shouting "Bravo!" How interesting. If it were an actor, they would have to buy many gramophones and record themselves shouting "Good!" to play when they go on stage.

But what happens if this kind of trick is exposed? There's a method for that too. Immediately put on a "pitiful" look and say that you have no party affiliation, don't borrow ideologies, and have no gang connections, "never daring to be arrogant," showing none of the head-shaking, tail-wagging, smug air of the "symposium" days. Instead, it seems like others are reactionaries, murderers, arsonists, Qing Gang, Red Gang, bullying this weak and talented young master.

What's even more effective is to say that his attacks are actually because his "ability is weak and unable to meet the demands of friends." If we didn't know the gender of this "writer," we would suspect that many people with party affiliations or gang connections have repeatedly borrowed money from him, or vehemently proposed to her, or something, and were "unable to satisfy" them, thus suffering unjust revenge.

But I hope my words still don't harm the "writer" of the "new era," and I'll "extract" a "good review" to use as a "substitute postscript":

'"Hiding it in famous mountains and passing it down to the right person" is long gone. In the twentieth century, there's a method. The liberation of lyrics, liberate, liberate, add flowers to brocade, how interesting? But others are reactionaries, bullying this weak and talented young master, actually because his "ability is weak and unable to meet the demands of friends," thus suffering unjust revenge, without harming the "writer" of the "new era."'

The Utmost in Kindness of Punishment and Reward 220

— Cao Juren

My friend, Mr. Muzhai, integrates the new and old, and is well-versed in ancient and modern times, making him worthy of respect and discussion. His discussion of "examination" says that we should learn from ancient methods and understand "punishment and reward." Even if Jia Yi and Dong Zhongshu were resurrected, they could only say so much.

Previous notes said that Emperor Taizong of Tang privately visited and was very pleased to see many successful new scholars (note) displaying their triumphant arrogance, saying, "All the heroes of the world have entered my snare!" The ancient method and meaning of the Chinese examination was originally to "bring all the heroes of the world into my snare." To wear down the youth's heroic ambitions under the lamplight, to gradually tame the wild wolf into a tail-wagging dog: from ancient times to the present, examinations have always emphasized essays and used Confucian classics; even though the Yuan and Qing entered China as barbarians, the power of the eight-legged essay and examination poems did not decline, that is the natural trend!

The great Northern Song writer Su Dongpo said in his famous provincial examination work, "On the Utmost in Kindness of Punishment and Reward," "The former kings knew that the goodness of the world could not be exhausted by rewards, and that titles and stipends were insufficient to encourage them; they knew that the evil of the world could not be exhausted by punishments, and that knives and saws were insufficient to cut them down. Therefore, they raised them and returned them to benevolence, treating the world with the way of gentlemen and elders, causing the world to follow them and return to the way of gentlemen and elders, hence it is said to be the utmost in kindness." The meaning is: it is natural for those with merit to receive high rewards; but there are too many merit dogs, and rewards cannot be exhausted, what should be done? It is also natural for reactionaries to be severely punished; but there are too many reactionaries, and punishments cannot be exhausted, what should be done? The former kings came up with a wonderful method, calling everyone to return to the way of gentlemen and elders, to return to the "benevolence" of the utmost in kindness. "Benevolence" is an abstract term, and when seen in action, a system called "imperial examination" is established. The meaning is: if you want high office and generous pay, then you should take the examination; if you want to take the examination, then you should follow my official procedures; if you follow my official procedures, then you will have to somersault in the sacred scriptures and virtuous biographies all your life; isn't this effect greater than rewarding with high office and generous pay, even though high office and generous pay are not used as a reward? If you don't take the examination, or if you take the examination but don't follow the official procedures, like Zhu Maichen living in poverty, or Su Qin failing the examination, the father doesn't consider him a son, the wife doesn't consider him a husband, the sister-in-law doesn't consider him an uncle, you can only hang yourself or prick your thigh and work hard again; isn't this effect better than punishing with knives and saws, even though knives and saws are not used as punishment? As the saying goes, "Teach your wife when she first comes, teach your child when he's a baby." In youth, first temper and refine, refine a good blank, if it is good, it will be enough to receive a high reward, and if it is bad, it will also avoid flowing into reaction, isn't this the utmost in kindness?

To cure an epidemic, you must use ancient prescriptions: to relieve stomach pain, please eat incense ash, and to treat malaria, you must recite the Gao Huang Sutra. We disciples of the sages can only save the country by reading the sutras! I further declare Su Zi's words to wait for the wind to be gathered by travelers!

(Note) The status of scholars in the Tang Dynasty was noble, slightly similar to that of Jinshi in the Ming and Qing Dynasties.

Night 221

— Miao Chongqun

After a summer, I returned to Nanjing again; now I am spending my second summer in Nanjing.

When I was away, whenever summer came, the thought of my father's illness, during this season, often evoked my melancholy and unease.

Now, I am still away, but my thoughts have become a blank. Summer has arrived, and my father's face, my father's flesh, my father's white beard, perhaps they will gradually decay and disappear in the coffin, right? It is this time of year.

When I parted with my younger brother, I said:

"Almost everyone who was the same age as our father has died. Now, only our generation is left."

Year after year has passed, and I don't know if my heart has become more lonely or more peaceful.

In the past, I seemed like a post horse, running from east to west, north and south, panting for a long time. Now, I don't know why, I'm dragging myself to whatever station it may be, and I need rest so much. When I arrive, I want to stay; in this one station, I want to rest forever.

This time when I returned to Nanjing, I no longer want to move. Because there is no comfortable place to stay, I simply squat in my wife's house, which is as big as a trough. I originally wanted to hold my breath here for two days, but to my surprise, an old friend whom I hadn't seen for a long time came to visit.

This trough is only so big, and he can only occupy a small army cot as his territory.

On summer nights, I often suffer from insomnia. Every night, after the oil lamp wick is turned low, they both sleep peacefully; and the lamp soon extinguishes itself as if it were tired.

I am restless, I listen attentively, but I can't hear a sound. The night is so dark and silent that I really don't know where I am resting.

An inexplicable restlessness causes an inexplicable itch on my body. An inexplicable itch causes an inexplicable restlessness in my heart.

I determined to strike a match, wanting to tear apart the darkness and silence of the night.

In the momentary light, I saw my old friend sleeping under the old wainscoting, and my wife sleeping beside me. On the white sheet, "Nanjing bugs" as big as pears were scurrying about busily.

The match went out, and the night returned to its darkness and silence.

Things that suck blood are in the dark.

My friend dreamed briefly from time to time.

My wife also dreamed briefly from time to time.

I asked them, but they didn't answer. I thought with horror: there is neither friend nor wife sleeping in this room. They are just two human forms, and they seem to be covered by ghosts.

Night is ghostly.

I still couldn't hear any sound. If the ash of the mosquito coil fell into the dish with a sound, it was heard by me.

I still couldn't see anything. If the little red ember of the mosquito coil was what I saw, then it undoubtedly was also watching the three of us.

I don't know how, I saw two embers of mosquito coils; the ghost seemed to have taken my hand, and I don't know how I got to the next morning.

The next morning, after they both woke up, I asked: "What did you dream about last night?"

"Nothing," they said with a smile, not remembering anything.

"Last night, I don't know why, but I saw two red embers in the mosquito coil dish," I asked, bringing up the mystery of the night.

"That was your illusion," my friend even denied what I saw.

···············

"For many years, friends like old friends have not increased."

My friend suddenly thought of such a sentence.

I was silent, thinking of what I said when I parted with my younger brother this time, and wanted to add:

"Our generation is also withering away as we watch."

Creative Fiction

Ordinary Matters (IV) 223

— Dan Guosun

"So, what to do?" Yongsun asked.

"They say they want to use the Changzhen Construction Company's name to provide relief to Zhabei."

The crowd seemed stunned to hear this. Yongsun sat up from the couch, propped himself up with his hands on the edge of the couch, and asked Botang with a puzzled expression:

Has the factory ever provided any relief before?

"The first time," Botang said, "they donated two hundred yuan in the name of consolation... The second time, they donated four hundred yuan worth of medicines and thirty bunk beds to the Red Cross. Last Wednesday, they also lent a truck used to transport materials to the local maintenance association to use."

"Then..." Yongsun drawled out the words, "Then... it can be considered that they have fulfilled some obligations... The matter... now... what should I say... to be good?... "

Everyone looked at Yongsun, who raised a hand and scratched his head for a while, and finally said:

"Botang, since they are coming tomorrow morning, let's talk about it again tomorrow morning!" At this time, the maid came in again:

"Mr. Zhang called, young master, and asked me to ask if the young master will be at the mansion tomorrow morning?"

"Which Mr. Zhang?" Botang asked.

"Mr. Zhang Ziyu, the person in charge of the factory. He said that he can't come out tonight without a notification."

Bokang did not answer, but stood up, walked out of the room, and went to the telephone to talk.

When he returned to the room, he saw that Yongsun had already put on his coat.

"Is Father leaving?"

"Yes, I'm leaving," Yongsun said, and then asked, "Does Zhiguang know about the factory's situation?"

"He knows a little bit, but not very clearly. He just got the information... Now, he will go to the factory early tomorrow morning and then come back..."

"That's good."

"Is Father coming back to stay here today?"

"I'm afraid not. There are many people staying here with you. If I don't come, I can take up one less bed, and everyone will be a little more comfortable!"

After Yongsun finished speaking, he looked at those who were taking refuge in Botang's house with a subtle smile. Botang asked:

"Where should we meet Father tomorrow?"

Yongsun thought for a while before saying:

"Listen for my call. It's really hard to say now... As for the factory's affairs, you can decide for yourself."

So he slowly left the door of this house, and the shadows of the people in the house followed him out one by one.

(II)

Eight or nine hours later, the weak gray light of dawn had slowly pierced the layer of thin mist covering the ten-mile foreign concession. At this time, the sound of artillery in the vicinity, as if following the usual practice of the past ten days or so, had stopped early as soon as it dawned. Although the sound of artillery in the distance was still faintly carried over by the northeast wind, it seemed that everyone in the foreign concession had forgotten at this time that they were lying behind the realistic battlefield around Zhabei: those who were fast asleep and had not woken up were still extending the sweet taste of last night, those who were using physical strength or power to move on the ground were busy with their daily lives, but those who opened their eyes and were on the bed or sitting on chairs were, at most, taking the daily newspaper published in the morning and shaking their heads and sighing!

However, what on earth was Yao Botang doing at this time?

Discourse

Today's Men of Letters 224

— Ben

In the past, in China, men of letters valued integrity very much. From the saying "A scholar can be killed but not humiliated," it can be known that ordinary men of letters generally had to maintain a certain amount of self-respect. For example, Li Taibai, such an uninhibited man of letters, his letter to Han Jingzhou was very solemn in attitude, neither arrogant nor humble, and the lines revealed a tough backbone of a man of letters. Ordinary men of letters were deeply influenced by the ancient sages' "learning leads to officialdom" and tempted by the feudal environment where men of letters had to enter officialdom, so of course everyone wanted to be an official, and everyone regarded being an official as the proper way out for a man of letters, but if they couldn't get it or were not satisfied with it, they would simply retreat to the countryside. Tao Qian is a good example.

Furthermore, when it comes to the relationship between men of letters, although there were divisions of factions and struggles between parties, they still paid attention to integrity. They encouraged each other's learning and conduct and rarely blindly praised each other or blindly attacked each other. It was even rarer for them to be as close as a ball of sealing wax for a short period of time, and then suddenly scold each other like village women, exhibiting all kinds of ugly behavior.

This, I think, is a common feeling shared by anyone who has read literary history or has a slight acquaintance with ancient literary works. I believe it is not something the author fabricates out of thin air.

History has evolved, and times have changed. When it comes to today's capitalist society, the bones and blood of men of letters seem to have changed their source. Integrity has been swept away, so it has provoked ordinary "indignant at the world and resentful of customs" moralistic elders to sigh in a long voice: "The world is deteriorating, and people's hearts are not as they used to be." In fact, society is constantly evolving. "The past" is not necessary. It is only "the world is deteriorating" and integrity is almost wiped out that is definitely not the phenomenon that the evolution of men of letters should have. It has led even children like the author to shout "It is worthy of a long sigh."

Today's men of letters, their desire to become officials is probably a thousand times stronger than that of the ancients, because there is a general situation of "more monks than congee" now. A man of letters relies entirely on the knowledge in his head. If he wants to squeeze in, it is simply not possible. Moreover, since the method of seeking officialdom by "singing praises and praising virtues" is no longer popular today, they have come up with wonderful ideas and further play the trick of auctioning off their souls. Thus, there are men of letters who were formerly proletarian writers who can transform themselves and grandly become county magistrates, and former ×× party members who are bought off and become supervisory officials in a matter of moments. This kind of person is numerous.

When men of letters get to this point, integrity has already disappeared.

And among men of letters, there is even more fickleness. If you are close to me today, I will blindly praise you. Tomorrow, I can regard you as an enemy, attacking you with all my strength. Forming alliances and cooperating one day, tearing down the platform and fighting the next. Switching sides is common, and all kinds of ugly behavior are displayed.

The tricks of today's men of letters are nothing more than this!

Facts tell us that the intellectual class has reached a period of decline, approaching the realm of the tomb. They do not talk about integrity at all, and are simply shameless. Perhaps it is the afterglow of the setting sun, the last scene of ugly struggle before death!

The Miracle of Early Summer 225

— Yu

It has been so slow in coming. I have not seen a single red peach or green willow in the atmosphere of the city, nor has a yellow oriole played with its tongue in front of my window; but the gentle breeze of early summer has already descended on the small building.

When I got up in the morning, I felt inexplicably uncomfortable all over. Without breakfast, I went to Avenue Joffre for a walk alone. Avenue Joffre and I were as intimate as old friends. When I stepped from books into society, for a full three years, my life was entrusted to Avenue Joffre. Now, due to environmental reasons, I moved from that romantic embrace into a narrow small building. When I return to Avenue Joffre, my spirit is uplifted. The shops that seemed familiar have been replaced with new posters; in just one year, only the small trees on the roadside are still fluttering in the morning breeze, but they have also grown a lot.

It was still early. The clear sky, the street cleaners dragging garbage trucks, walking slowly with their heads down, as if they were in a fairyland. I counted the squares of the sidewalk and floated along. My steps were so slow, and I was whistling a popular song about a lover in my dream, walking without knowing why. In the distance, a young woman in a white silk dress was pushing a baby carriage towards me. She was leisurely and lightly tilting her head, as if teasing her little darling. A smile slipped from the corner of her mouth, and her temples were flying in the morning breeze.

We met face to face in front of a beautiful window display. With a familiar outline, I avoided her gaze and brushed past her, but I didn't want to walk far, so I secretly turned my eyes back. She was leaning back on the back of the carriage with both hands, watching my back.

"Miss Ling," rolled in my throat.

"Mr. Zhang, is that you!" She jumped over, dragging the baby carriage.

"Although your face is familiar, I don't recognize you."

A smile slipped from the corner of her mouth, and her temples were flying in the morning breeze.

"Still at the Russian woman's house?"

"No, just walking around."

"Going to the French Park?"

I pushed the baby carriage, and the child smiled at me.

"Is this yours?"

She nodded, and a virgin's blush appeared on her cheeks.

When I lived in the Russian woman's house, I met Miss Ling. She was still a mischievous child of fifteen, eating chocolate and playing with a ball. Because I was a lonely person, I was very happy to have an innocent companion. One day, in the French Park, I inadvertently asked her: "Do you want to study?" She said she didn't have any money, so I agreed to teach her. From the next day, she came to my residence to study every night.

In summer, we met in the French Park in the morning, and teaching was also changed to that time, in the thatched pavilion at the entrance. Because I also worked at a night club at night.

Miss Ling was very smart, and she could already distinguish the use of I and Me. Also on a sunny day, before teaching, she asked me what the pronunciation of "love" was. "Love," I said.

Ni Gaoshi's Liangchang Thatched Cottage Ziju's Nostril Breathing Out, Occasionally Imitating the General Idea, Xinwei August, Painted for Miss Pei Fang, Daughter of Disuo, and Kindly Requested for Admonishment by the Old Man Wu Hufan Chouyi

Mr. Wu Hufan's Painting (Brief Biography)

Wu Hufan, alias Chouyi, is the grandson of the Prime Minister of Kezhai. He inherited the family's learning early and had already established an outstanding reputation in his youth. The literati and officials in Wuzhong all liked to make friends with him, but his theory of painting was not based on the old ways. His brushwork could create a painting even when upside down and in disarray. His intelligence was so supreme that it was beyond the reach of ordinary people.

"For example, I love you is I Love you, and you love me is You Love Me."

"Correct."

She smiled, and a virgin's blush appeared on her cheeks. We pushed the car, side by side, and entered the gate of the French Park. I looked up and saw a middle-aged man teaching a girl to read in the thatched pavilion.

We walked slowly, floating along, under the trees, by the river, sadly reminiscing.

She is now someone else's wife, a child's mother, no longer eating chocolate or playing with a ball; even less can I hear her say "Love You, You Love Me."

We walked slowly, floating along, under the trees, by the river, sadly reminiscing.

We left the French Park, pushing the car, side by side, and parted ways in front of the beautiful window display.

"See you tomorrow!"

"Goodbye."

A young woman in a white silk dress was pushing a baby carriage away from me.

A smile slipped from the corner of her mouth, and her temples were flying in the morning breeze.

Staff Correspondence 227

What is the purpose of life?

Dear Editor:

I have a question, namely, "What is the purpose of life?" I previously read Liang Rengong's posthumous work, which had an essay on this topic; but it never answered the ultimate question, and I have been doubtful ever since. I am shallow and unlearned, and I dare not make reckless comments. Now, thanks to my two friends, Ye and Wei, who do not abandon my ignorance, they have answered for me, saying, "The purpose of life is, in the final analysis, to eat." The two gentlemen also cited Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People, which emphasizes people's livelihood, and the Principle of People's Livelihood has a special section on the issue of eating, arguing vigorously to the extreme. The two gentlemen cited the current economic panic, social crisis, and unemployment problems, all of which are directly or indirectly related to the issue of eating, as evidence. A difficult problem that has not been resolved for more than ten years has been solved by the two gentlemen, how happy! However, when I think about it in the quiet of the night, it seems that their words are not exhaustive, so I respectfully send this letter to you for instruction, and I would be extremely grateful if you would give me final guidance. I respectfully wish you

Peace, Liu Xingchuan respectfully 228

○　○　○　○

Editor's Note: The purpose of life is simply the word "live." Even ants greedily cling to life, let alone humans. Within the meaning of this word "live," there are two elements: 1. How to be able to live, and 2. How to live meaningfully. Those who have no way to solve the first problem have no time and should not bother with the second problem. However, once you have solved the first problem, you cannot but attempt to take the second step. Because if you don't, you will lose the original driving force of life. If the first problem is not solved, you will inevitably be forced to commit suicide; if the second problem is not solved, you will become tired of the world; although the forms are different, they both result in the inability to survive. Before the material competition was eased, of course, some people said, "The purpose of life is to establish merit and achieve success"; in this era of sharpened survival competition, it is certainly possible to say, "The purpose of life is to eat." However, society is unequal. When it is not a problem for the masses to eat, it is hard to guarantee that there will not be a minority who have no way to make a living; similarly, in the current situation where the lives of the masses cannot be maintained, there are also a very small number of bourgeoisie. Therefore, we still believe that the purpose of life is the word "live"; "how to be able to live" and "how to live meaningfully" are both indispensable.

Market News 229

The Effectiveness of Stinky Water: Stinky water is a necessity for the summer season. Whenever it is sprinkled in deep ditches and remote places, epidemics will be eliminated immediately. Among domestic products, the Double Knife brand from Xinyuan Company and Yalin Antiepidemic Water from Wuzhou Pharmacy are the most popular.

Beware of Inferior Toys: Recently, many rubber toys have appeared on the market, such as balls, birds, animals, etc. The peddlers are selling them all day long. After investigation, these products have no business name, and they are obviously Japanese goods. Please pay special attention and do not be deceived. Domestic toys that are similar to this item are only sold by Chen Jiageng Company, but the products have a Chinese trademark. Rubber balls are only sold by Yonghe Industrial Company, and the styles are completely different, and there is a "Yong" trademark as a mark.

Fiction

Under the Traffic Lights (20) 230

— Xilin

"Aren't you going?" Third Mistress Tai shouted.

"But, I haven't eaten yet?" He wanted to use this reason to decline.

"I was just thinking of having some refreshments, so I'll accompany you to a Western restaurant nearby!" Third Mistress Tai pressed him so tightly, the pride of a woman made her determined to take him away from Meizi's side.

Then, she deliberately affectionately took Shi Qiao's arm. And so, they walked slowly side by side towards the garden, like a young couple.

"That landlady is a Japanese woman, aren't you the most hateful of Japanese people?" Third Mistress said in a low voice, "Hey, one can imagine that what you say about patriotism is also fake."

Of course, there was no need for him to argue with such shallow and childish words, and the more important problem was that he didn't have a penny to eat at the Western restaurant. Of course, Third Mistress Tai wouldn't think of this, and continued, "The Japanese are, after all, not easy to mess with! Moreover, the Russians are staying in the house all day long!"

"Hey! Why don't you say a word? Are you angry?" ││ "Have I been bad to you in any way? Tell me, tell me!"

Treating him to meals, accompanying him to dances, and letting him... of course, she was good to him. How could he answer this?

Fortunately, on the other side of the pavement, Wang Hua was walking towards him with someone else. From far away, he shouted:

"Shi Qiao, Shi Qiao! Where are you going, where are you going?"

When they got close, the person who came with him was Hu Yuanliang, a tall, skinny man, and Shi Qiao hadn't seen him for a long time. Wang Hua had changed into a very neat Western suit, and even his hair was combed slickly. Although he wasn't handsome enough to be called a pretty boy, he was a typical little swindler. He secretly whispered to Shi Qiao:

"Please introduce me!"

"Oh, yes, this is Mr. Wang Hua, and this is Mr. Hu Yuanliang." Shi Qiao then pointed to Third Mistress Tai: "This is Miss, Miss Li!"

"Oh, so you are from the same family! Excellent, excellent." These words were of course said by Wang Hua. Then he leaned closer to Shi Qiao's ear:

"Hello, hello!" │ "Look, we are going to start formal activities. Look, I specially borrowed a suit to wear today. You should always dress nicely when you are active. The most taboo is to look poor! Yuanliang completely agrees with our affairs, Yuanliang!"

The tall, skinny man had to come up and exchange a few pleasantries with Shi Qiao.

"We'll come to your house again tonight! Goodbye. Miss Li!"

Wang the dwarf led Hu the skinny and bowed respectfully.
